//  rawaf-setup.js — Rawaf Dashboard Auto-Setup Script
//  Run: node rawaf-setup.js
//  This script creates all source files and installs deps.
// ============================================================
const fs   = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const { execSync } = require('child_process');

function write(rel, content) {
  const abs = path.resolve(rel);
  fs.mkdirSync(path.dirname(abs), { recursive: true });
  fs.writeFileSync(abs, content, 'utf8');
  console.log('  ✓', rel);
}

console.log('
🚀 Rawaf Dashboard — إعداد تلقائي

write("artifacts/rawaf-dashboard/src/App.tsx", "import { useState, useEffect } from \"react\";\nimport \"./index.css\";\nimport Header from \"./components/Header\";\nimport MainDashboard from \"./components/MainDashboard\";\nimport DatabasePage from \"./components/DatabasePage\";\nimport SplashGate from \"./components/SplashGate\";\nimport { EMPTY_FILTERS, type FilterState } from \"./components/filterTypes\";\nimport { ContractorsProvider } from \"./contractors/context\";\n\nexport type TabType = \"main\" | \"database\";\n\nexport interface CurrentUser {\n  id: number;\n  name: string;\n  loginName: string;\n  jobTitle: string;\n  role: string;\n  isActive: number;\n  lastActive: string | null;\n  createdAt: string;\n}\n\nfunction readCurrentUser(): CurrentUser | null {\n  try {\n    const s = sessionStorage.getItem(\"rawaf_current_user\");\n    return s ? (JSON.parse(s) as CurrentUser) : null;\n  } catch { return null; }\n}\n\nfunction App() {\n  const [activeTab, setActiveTab]     = useState<TabType>(\"main\");\n  const [search, setSearch]           = useState(\"\");\n  const [selectedId, setSelectedId]   = useState<number | null>(null);\n  const [filters, setFilters]         = useState<FilterState>(EMPTY_FILTERS);\n  const [currentUser, setCurrentUser] = useState<CurrentUser | null>(readCurrentUser);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const onLogin = (e: Event) => {\n      const user = (e as CustomEvent<CurrentUser>).detail;\n      setCurrentUser(user);\n      if (user.role === \"user\") setActiveTab(\"main\");\n    };\n    const onLogout = () => setCurrentUser(null);\n    const onProfileUpdated = (e: Event) => {\n      const user = (e as CustomEvent<CurrentUser>).detail;\n      setCurrentUser(user);\n      sessionStorage.setItem(\"rawaf_current_user\", JSON.stringify(user));\n    };\n    window.addEventListener(\"rawaf-login\",           onLogin          as EventListener);\n    window.addEventListener(\"rawaf-logout\",          onLogout         as EventListener);\n    window.addEventListener(\"rawaf-profile-updated\", onProfileUpdated as EventListener);\n    return () => {\n      window.removeEventListener(\"rawaf-login\",           onLogin          as EventListener);\n      window.removeEventListener(\"rawaf-logout\",          onLogout         as EventListener);\n      window.removeEventListener(\"rawaf-profile-updated\", onProfileUpdated as EventListener);\n    };\n  }, []);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!currentUser) return;\n    const ping = () =>\n      fetch(\"/api/auth/heartbeat\", {\n        method: \"POST\",\n        headers: { \"Content-Type\": \"application/json\" },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ loginName: currentUser.loginName }),\n      }).catch(() => {});\n    void ping();\n    const t = setInterval(() => void ping(), 60_000);\n    return () => clearInterval(t);\n  }, [currentUser]);\n\n  // Hide page scrollbar on welcome state (no search / filter / selection)\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const hasAnyFilter = Object.values(filters).some(v => v !== \"\");\n    const isWelcome = activeTab === \"main\" && !search.trim() && !selectedId && !hasAnyFilter;\n    document.body.classList.toggle(\"welcome-state\", isWelcome);\n    return () => { document.body.classList.remove(\"welcome-state\"); };\n  }, [activeTab, search, selectedId, filters]);\n\n  function handleSearchChange(value: string) {\n    setSearch(value);\n    setSelectedId(null);\n  }\n\n  function handleFiltersChange(f: FilterState) {\n    // itemPrice is comparison-only — don't reset the selected contractor when only it changes\n    const onlyPriceChanged =\n      f.itemPrice !== filters.itemPrice &&\n      f.contractor      === filters.contractor      &&\n      f.portfolio       === filters.portfolio       &&\n      f.mainActivity    === filters.mainActivity    &&\n      f.businessProgram === filters.businessProgram &&\n      f.workFamily      === filters.workFamily      &&\n      f.workType        === filters.workType        &&\n      f.workCategory    === filters.workCategory    &&\n      f.itemScope       === filters.itemScope       &&\n      f.techSpecs       === filters.techSpecs       &&\n      f.measurements    === filters.measurements;\n    setFilters(f);\n    if (!onlyPriceChanged) setSelectedId(null);\n  }\n\n  const isWelcome = activeTab === \"main\" && !search.trim() && !selectedId && !Object.values(filters).some(v => v !== \"\");\n\n  return (\n    <SplashGate>\n      <ContractorsProvider>\n        <div style={{\n          ...(isWelcome ? { height: \"100vh\", overflow: \"hidden\" } : { minHeight: \"100vh\" }),\n          display: \"flex\", flexDirection: \"column\",\n          backgroundColor: \"var(--body-bg)\",\n        }}>\n          <Header\n            activeTab={activeTab}\n            onTabChange={setActiveTab}\n            search={search}\n            onSearchChange={handleSearchChange}\n            filters={filters}\n            onFiltersChange={handleFiltersChange}\n            currentUser={currentUser}\n          />\n          <div key={activeTab} style={{ flex: 1, minHeight: 0 }}>\n            {activeTab === \"main\" ? (\n              <MainDashboard\n                search={search}\n                filters={filters}\n                selectedId={selectedId}\n                onSelectId={setSelectedId}\n              />\n            ) : (\n              <DatabasePage\n                search={search}\n                filters={filters}\n                onFiltersChange={handleFiltersChange}\n                currentUser={currentUser}\n                onSelectContractor={(id) => { setSelectedId(id); setActiveTab(\"main\"); }}\n              />\n            )}\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      </ContractorsProvider>\n    </SplashGate>\n  );\n}\n\nexport default App;\n");
write("artifacts/rawaf-dashboard/src/main.tsx", "import { createRoot } from \"react-dom/client\";\nimport { QueryClient, QueryClientProvider } from \"@tanstack/react-query\";\nimport App from \"./App\";\nimport \"./index.css\";\n\nconst queryClient = new QueryClient({\n  defaultOptions: {\n    queries: { retry: 2, staleTime: 30_000 },\n  },\n});\n\ncreateRoot(document.getElementById(\"root\")!).render(\n  <QueryClientProvider client={queryClient}>\n    <App />\n  </QueryClientProvider>\n);\n");

write("artifacts/rawaf-dashboard/src/components/MainDashboard.tsx", "import { useContractorsContext } from \"../contractors/context\";\nimport Sidebar from \"./Sidebar\";\nimport MainContent from \"./MainContent\";\nimport WelcomeHero from \"./WelcomeHero\";\nimport type { Contractor } from \"../contractors/types\";\nimport type { FilterState } from \"./filterTypes\";\n\ninterface Props {\n  search:      string;\n  filters:     FilterState;\n  selectedId:  number | null;\n  onSelectId:  (id: number) => void;\n}\n\nfunction normalize(s: string) {\n  return (s ?? \"\")\n    .replace(/[\\u064B-\\u065F]/g, \"\")\n    .replace(/[أإآ]/g, \"ا\")\n    .replace(/ة/g, \"ه\")\n    .replace(/ى/g, \"ي\")\n    .toLowerCase()\n    .trim();\n}\n\nfunction contractorMatchesSearch(c: Contractor, search: string): boolean {\n  if (!search) return false;\n  const n = normalize(search);\n  return (\n    normalize(c.contractNo).includes(n)                      ||\n    normalize(c.contractYear    ?? \"\").includes(n)           ||\n    normalize(c.contractor).includes(n)                      ||\n    normalize(c.project).includes(n)                         ||\n    normalize(c.portfolio).includes(n)                       ||\n    normalize(c.technicalScope).includes(n)                  ||\n    normalize(c.workType).includes(n)                        ||\n    normalize(c.workCategory    ?? \"\").includes(n)           ||\n    normalize(c.mainActivity    ?? \"\").includes(n)           ||\n    normalize(c.businessProgram ?? \"\").includes(n)           ||\n    normalize(c.workFamily      ?? \"\").includes(n)           ||\n    normalize(c.itemScope       ?? \"\").includes(n)           ||\n    normalize(c.itemCode        ?? \"\").includes(n)           ||\n    normalize(c.techSpecs       ?? \"\").includes(n)           ||\n    normalize(c.measurements    ?? \"\").includes(n)           ||\n    normalize(c.unit            ?? \"\").includes(n)           ||\n    normalize(c.phone           ?? \"\").includes(n)           ||\n    normalize(c.workScopeText   ?? \"\").includes(n)\n  );\n}\n\nfunction contractorMatchesFilters(c: Contractor, filters: FilterState): boolean {\n  if (filters.contractor      && normalize(c.contractor)              !== normalize(filters.contractor))      return false;\n  if (filters.portfolio       && normalize(c.portfolio)               !== normalize(filters.portfolio))       return false;\n  if (filters.mainActivity    && normalize(c.mainActivity    ?? \"\")   !== normalize(filters.mainActivity))    return false;\n  if (filters.businessProgram && normalize(c.businessProgram ?? \"\")   !== normalize(filters.businessProgram)) return false;\n  if (filters.workFamily      && normalize(c.workFamily      ?? \"\")   !== normalize(filters.workFamily))      return false;\n  if (filters.workType        && normalize(c.workType)                !== normalize(filters.workType))        return false;\n  if (filters.workCategory    && normalize(c.workCategory    ?? \"\")   !== normalize(filters.workCategory))    return false;\n  if (filters.itemScope       && normalize(c.itemScope       ?? \"\")   !== normalize(filters.itemScope))       return false;\n  if (filters.techSpecs       && normalize(c.techSpecs       ?? \"\")   !== normalize(filters.techSpecs))       return false;\n  if (filters.measurements    && normalize(c.measurements    ?? \"\")   !== normalize(filters.measurements))    return false;\n  return true;\n}\n\nexport default function MainDashboard({ search, filters, selectedId, onSelectId }: Props) {\n  const { data: allContractors = [], isLoading } = useContractorsContext();\n\n  const hasSearch       = search.trim().length > 0;\n  // itemPrice is comparison-only — exclude it from sidebar filtering logic\n  const hasFilters      = Object.entries(filters).some(([key, val]) => key !== \"itemPrice\" && Boolean(val));\n  const hasDirectSelect = selectedId != null;\n\n  // Identify the directly selected contractor\n  const directRecord = hasDirectSelect\n    ? allContractors.find((c: Contractor) => c.id === selectedId)\n    : undefined;\n\n  // Filtered list for the sidebar:\n  //  - Searching / filtering → matches\n  //  - Direct select (from DB) → similar items by family+type+scope hierarchy\n  //  - Idle → empty (WelcomeHero)\n  let filtered: Contractor[];\n  if (hasSearch || hasFilters) {\n    filtered = allContractors.filter((c: Contractor) => {\n      const matchesSearch  = hasSearch  ? contractorMatchesSearch(c, search.trim()) : true;\n      const matchesFilters = hasFilters ? contractorMatchesFilters(c, filters)     : true;\n      return matchesSearch && matchesFilters;\n    });\n  } else if (hasDirectSelect && directRecord) {\n    const n = (s: string) => (s ?? \"\").replace(/[\\u064B-\\u065F]/g, \"\").replace(/[أإآ]/g, \"ا\").replace(/ة/g, \"ه\").replace(/ى/g, \"ي\").toLowerCase().trim();\n    const family = n(directRecord.workFamily ?? \"\");\n    const type   = n(directRecord.workType);\n    const scope  = n(directRecord.itemScope  ?? \"\");\n\n    // L1: family + type + scope\n    if (family && type && scope) {\n      const pool = allContractors.filter((c: Contractor) =>\n        n(c.workFamily ?? \"\") === family && n(c.workType) === type && n(c.itemScope ?? \"\") === scope\n      );\n      if (pool.length > 0) { filtered = pool; }\n      else if (family && type) {\n        // L2: family + type\n        const pool2 = allContractors.filter((c: Contractor) =>\n          n(c.workFamily ?? \"\") === family && n(c.workType) === type\n        );\n        filtered = pool2.length > 0 ? pool2 : allContractors.filter((c: Contractor) => n(c.workType) === type);\n      } else {\n        filtered = allContractors.filter((c: Contractor) => n(c.workType) === type);\n      }\n    } else if (family && type) {\n      // L2: family + type\n      const pool2 = allContractors.filter((c: Contractor) =>\n        n(c.workFamily ?? \"\") === family && n(c.workType) === type\n      );\n      filtered = pool2.length > 0 ? pool2 : allContractors.filter((c: Contractor) => n(c.workType) === type);\n    } else {\n      // L3: type only\n      filtered = allContractors.filter((c: Contractor) => n(c.workType) === type);\n    }\n  } else {\n    filtered = [];\n  }\n\n  // Always resolve selectedId from the FULL dataset.\n  const selected: Contractor | null =\n    selectedId != null\n      ? (allContractors.find((c: Contractor) => c.id === selectedId) ?? null)\n      : filtered[0] ?? null;\n\n  // Is the selected contractor part of the current filter result?\n  // If not (e.g. navigated via work-history from outside the filter),\n  // fall back to allContractors so price comparison stays meaningful.\n  const selectedInFiltered = selected != null && filtered.some((c: Contractor) => c.id === selected.id);\n\n  const hasNoSearchResults = (hasSearch || hasFilters) && filtered.length === 0;\n\n  // Show welcome only when truly idle — no search, no filters, no direct selection\n  if (!hasSearch && !hasFilters && !hasDirectSelect && !isLoading) {\n    return <WelcomeHero />;\n  }\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"main-grid\">\n      <Sidebar\n        filtered={filtered}\n        allContractors={allContractors}\n        selectedId={selected?.id ?? null}\n        onSelect={onSelectId}\n        isLoading={isLoading}\n        hasFilter={hasSearch || hasFilters || hasDirectSelect}\n      />\n      <MainContent\n        contractor={selected}\n        allContractors={allContractors}\n        filteredContractors={filtered}\n        isLoading={isLoading}\n        onSelectId={onSelectId}\n        customPrice={filters.itemPrice ? Number(filters.itemPrice) : null}\n        emptyStateMessage={hasNoSearchResults ? \"لا توجد نتائج مطابقة لهذا البحث أو الفلتر\" : undefined}\n      />\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n");
write("artifacts/rawaf-dashboard/src/components/MainContent.tsx", "import { useState, useEffect, useRef } from \"react\";\nimport { Building2, Mail, Phone, FileText, Briefcase, MapPin, DollarSign, Clock } from \"lucide-react\";\nimport type { Contractor } from \"../contractors/types\";\n\ninterface Props {\n  contractor: Contractor | null;\n  allContractors: Contractor[];\n  filteredContractors: Contractor[];\n  isLoading: boolean;\n  onSelectId: (id: number) => void;\n  customPrice?: number | null;\n  emptyStateMessage?: string;\n}\n\nconst BAR_COLORS = [\"#2baa74\", \"#c5a059\", \"#3b8fcc\", \"#e8851c\", \"#9b59b6\", \"#e74c3c\"];\n\nfunction normalize(s: string) {\n  return (s ?? \"\")\n    .replace(/[\\u064B-\\u065F]/g, \"\")\n    .replace(/[أإآ]/g, \"ا\")\n    .replace(/ة/g, \"ه\")\n    .replace(/ى/g, \"ي\")\n    .toLowerCase()\n    .trim();\n}\n\nfunction formatExact(p: number) {\n  if (p == null) return \"—\";\n  return p.toLocaleString(\"en\");\n}\n\nfunction avg(arr: number[]) {\n  return arr.length ? arr.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / arr.length : 0;\n}\n\n/** Inline read-only stars — shown next to contractor name */\nfunction StarInline({ rating }: { rating?: number | null }) {\n  const r = Math.max(0, Math.min(5, Math.round(rating ?? 0)));\n  if (r === 0) return null;\n  return (\n    <span style={{ display: \"inline-flex\", gap: \"1px\", alignItems: \"center\", verticalAlign: \"middle\" }}>\n      {[1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map((i) => (\n        <span\n          key={i}\n          style={{\n            fontSize: \"0.8rem\",\n            color: i <= r ? \"#f5c518\" : \"rgba(255,255,255,0.2)\",\n            lineHeight: 1,\n            filter: i <= r ? \"drop-shadow(0 0 2px rgba(245,197,24,0.5))\" : \"none\",\n          }}\n        >★</span>\n      ))}\n      <span style={{ fontSize: \"0.58rem\", color: \"rgba(255,255,255,0.4)\", marginRight: \"3px\" }}>\n        {r}/5\n      </span>\n    </span>\n  );\n}\n\nfunction TruncatedBadge({\n  value,\n  title,\n}: {\n  value: string;\n  title?: string;\n}) {\n  return (\n    <span\n      title={title ?? value}\n      style={{\n        display: \"block\",\n        minWidth: 0,\n        overflow: \"hidden\",\n        whiteSpace: \"nowrap\",\n        textOverflow: \"ellipsis\",\n        direction: \"rtl\",\n        position: \"relative\",\n        zIndex: 1,\n      }}\n    >\n      {value}\n    </span>\n  );\n}\n\n/* ── 3-Tier comparison based on the numeric digit portion of the item code ──\n   Code format: `<L>-<16 digits>` where the 16 digits are 8 slots×2.\n   Portfolio letter is intentionally EXCLUDED from all tier comparisons so\n   contractors across all portfolios compete in the same price pool.\n   Tier 1 (دقيق):    all 16 digits match               → identical item (incl. نوع التعاقد)\n   Tier 2 (متماثل):  first 6 slots (12 digits) match   → same scope/type (excl. نوع التعاقد)\n   Tier 3 (موسّع):   first 3 slots (6 digits) match    → same work family\n*/\ntype Tier = \"exact\" | \"similar\" | \"broad\";\n\nconst TIER_META: Record<Tier, { label: string; icon: string; color: string; slots: number; tip: string }> = {\n  exact:   { label: \"دقيق\",   icon: \"🎯\", color: \"#2baa74\", slots: 8, tip: \"تطابق كامل لجميع حقول الكود بما فيها نوع التعاقد — أعدل مقارنة\" },\n  similar: { label: \"متماثل\", icon: \"⚖️\", color: \"#c5a059\", slots: 6, tip: \"تطابق النشاط + البرنامج + العائلة + نوع الأعمال + الشمولية + المواصفات\" },\n  broad:   { label: \"موسّع\",  icon: \"🌐\", color: \"#3b8fcc\", slots: 3, tip: \"تطابق النشاط + البرنامج + العائلة\" },\n};\n\n/** Extract only the digit portion of an item code (strips the portfolio letter prefix). */\nfunction codeDigits(code: string | null | undefined): string {\n  if (!code) return \"\";\n  const dash = code.indexOf(\"-\");\n  return dash !== -1 ? code.slice(dash + 1) : code;\n}\n\n/** Return the first `slots*2` digits of the digit portion for prefix matching. */\nfunction codeDigitsPrefix(code: string | null | undefined, slots: number): string {\n  const digits = codeDigits(code);\n  const want   = slots * 2;\n  return digits.length >= want ? digits.slice(0, want) : \"\";\n}\n\nfunction codePrefix(code: string | null | undefined, slots: number): string {\n  if (!code) return \"\";\n  const want = 2 + slots * 2; // \"L-\" + slots×2 digits\n  return code.length >= want ? code.slice(0, want) : \"\";\n}\n\nfunction buildMask(code: string | null | undefined, slots: number): string {\n  if (!code) return \"—\";\n  const prefix    = codePrefix(code, slots);\n  const remaining = Math.max(0, 16 - slots * 2);\n  return prefix + \"_\".repeat(remaining);\n}\n\nexport default function MainContent({ contractor, allContractors, filteredContractors, isLoading, onSelectId, customPrice, emptyStateMessage }: Props) {\n  // Active stat tab index (0=custom/current, 1=min, 2=avg, 3=max)\n  const [activeStat, setActiveStat] = useState(0);\n  // Prevents resetting activeStat when contractor change was triggered by clicking a stat cell\n  const skipStatReset = useRef(false);\n  // Cycle indices for min / avg / max cells\n  const [minCycleIdx, setMinCycleIdx] = useState(0);\n  const [avgCycleIdx, setAvgCycleIdx] = useState(0);\n  const [maxCycleIdx, setMaxCycleIdx] = useState(0);\n  // Comparison tier — null means \"auto-pick the most precise tier with ≥2 records\"\n  const [userTier, setUserTier] = useState<Tier | null>(null);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (skipStatReset.current) { skipStatReset.current = false; return; }\n    setActiveStat(customPrice && customPrice > 0 ? 2 : 0);\n    setMinCycleIdx(0);\n    setAvgCycleIdx(0);\n    setMaxCycleIdx(0);\n    setUserTier(null); // reset to auto-pick on contractor change\n  }, [contractor?.id]);\n  // When a custom price is entered for the first time, highlight the \"السعر المقارن\" cell (index 0)\n  const prevCustomPrice = useRef<number | null | undefined>(null);\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const had = prevCustomPrice.current && prevCustomPrice.current > 0;\n    const has  = customPrice && customPrice > 0;\n    if (has && !had) setActiveStat(0);\n    if (!has && had) setActiveStat(0);\n    prevCustomPrice.current = customPrice;\n  }, [customPrice]);\n\n  if (isLoading) {\n    return (\n      <main className=\"content-area\">\n        {[1, 2, 3].map((n) => (\n          <div key={n} style={{ background: \"#fff\", borderRadius: \"16px\", height: \"140px\", marginBottom: \"16px\", animation: \"pulse-gold 1.5s ease-in-out infinite\" }} />\n        ))}\n      </main>\n    );\n  }\n\n  // ── Price pools: 3-tier hierarchical match driven by the unique item code ──\n  // Portfolio letter is IGNORED in all tiers — only the 14 digit portion is\n  // compared, so contractors across different portfolios compete together.\n  // Tier 1 (exact):   all 14 digits match           → identical item\n  // Tier 2 (similar): first 5 slots (10 digits)     → same scope/type\n  // Tier 3 (broad):   first 3 slots (6 digits)      → same work family\n  // Legacy fallback: when the current record has no itemCode, fall back to\n  // text-based workType matching (so old data stays comparable).\n  const currentCode    = (contractor as any)?.itemCode as string | null | undefined;\n  const hasCode        = !!currentCode;\n  const currentDigits  = codeDigits(currentCode);\n  const digitsPrefix5  = codeDigitsPrefix(currentCode, 5);\n  const digitsPrefix3  = codeDigitsPrefix(currentCode, 3);\n\n  const workTypeKey   = contractor ? normalize(contractor.workType) : \"\";\n  const legacyPool: Contractor[] = (!hasCode && workTypeKey)\n    ? filteredContractors.filter((c) => normalize(c.workType) === workTypeKey)\n    : [];\n\n  const poolExact: Contractor[] = hasCode && currentDigits\n    ? filteredContractors.filter((c) => {\n        const d = codeDigits((c as any).itemCode);\n        return !!d && d === currentDigits;\n      })\n    : legacyPool;\n  const poolSimilar: Contractor[] = hasCode && digitsPrefix5\n    ? filteredContractors.filter((c) => {\n        const d = codeDigits((c as any).itemCode);\n        return !!d && d.startsWith(digitsPrefix5);\n      })\n    : legacyPool;\n  const poolBroad: Contractor[] = hasCode && digitsPrefix3\n    ? filteredContractors.filter((c) => {\n        const d = codeDigits((c as any).itemCode);\n        return !!d && d.startsWith(digitsPrefix3);\n      })\n    : legacyPool;\n\n  const tierPools: Record<Tier, Contractor[]> = {\n    exact:   poolExact,\n    similar: poolSimilar,\n    broad:   poolBroad,\n  };\n\n  // Auto-pick starting from \"متماثل\" (similar) — wide enough to show a\n  // meaningful market sample, yet still scoped to the same work type.\n  // Falls back to broad if similar has fewer than 2 records, or to exact\n  // as a last resort when only identical items exist.\n  const autoTier: Tier =\n    poolSimilar.length >= 2 ? \"similar\"\n    : poolBroad.length   >= 2 ? \"broad\"\n    : poolExact.length   >= 2 ? \"exact\"\n    : \"similar\";\n  const tier: Tier = userTier ?? autoTier;\n\n  let pricePool: Contractor[] = tierPools[tier];\n  if (pricePool.length === 0 && contractor) pricePool = [contractor];\n\n  const scopePoolSize = pricePool.length;\n\n  // Mask ribbon for the active tier — shows which digits are \"fixed\" vs free.\n  const tierMask  = buildMask(currentCode, TIER_META[tier].slots);\n  const tierMeta  = TIER_META[tier];\n  // Human-readable scope label (shown in the dark footer header)\n  const poolLabel: string = !contractor\n    ? \"—\"\n    : tier === \"exact\"\n      ? (currentCode || contractor.workType || \"—\")\n      : tier === \"similar\"\n        ? `${contractor.workFamily ?? \"\"} › ${contractor.workType ?? \"\"} › ${contractor.itemScope ?? \"\"}`.replace(/^›|›$/g, \"\").trim()\n        : `${contractor.mainActivity ?? \"\"} › ${contractor.workFamily ?? \"\"}`.replace(/^›|›$/g, \"\").trim();\n\n  // Only consider records with a valid price > 0 for min/max/avg calculations\n  const validPricePool = pricePool.filter((c) => c.price > 0);\n  const allPrices      = validPricePool.map((c) => c.price);\n  const maxPrice       = allPrices.length > 0 ? Math.max(...allPrices) : 1;\n  const minPrice       = allPrices.length > 0 ? Math.min(...allPrices) : 0;\n  const avgPrice       = avg(allPrices);\n\n  // ── Price under evaluation ─────────────────────────────────────────────\n  //    Use the user-entered custom price when present (an external offer\n  //    being benchmarked), otherwise the current contractor's stored price.\n  //    All deviation/ranking logic below pivots on this single value so\n  //    custom offers are scored against the internal tier pool exactly the\n  //    same way the contractor's own price is.\n  const hasCustomPrice = !!(customPrice && customPrice > 0);\n  const priceUnderEval = hasCustomPrice ? (customPrice as number) : (contractor?.price ?? 0);\n  const evalLabel      = hasCustomPrice ? \"السعر المُدخل\" : \"سعر المقاول الحالي\";\n\n  // ── Price-deviation alarm: when the price under evaluation diverges\n  //    from the tier's average by more than 30%, flip the tier indicator\n  //    to red regardless of which tier is active (financial-protection rule).\n  const deviationPct = (priceUnderEval > 0 && avgPrice > 0)\n    ? Math.abs(priceUnderEval - avgPrice) / avgPrice\n    : 0;\n  const isHighDeviation = deviationPct > 0.30 && validPricePool.length >= 2;\n  const activeTierColor = isHighDeviation ? \"#e74c3c\" : tierMeta.color;\n\n  // ── Rank of the evaluated price inside the current tier ────────────────\n  //    `cheaperCount` = how many tier records strictly undercut us.\n  //    Rank = cheaperCount + 1.  Useful both for the contractor's own\n  //    price AND for benchmarking an externally-typed offer.\n  const cheaperCount = validPricePool.filter((c) => c.price < priceUnderEval).length;\n  const evalRank     = priceUnderEval > 0 ? cheaperCount + 1 : 0;\n  const evalTotal    = validPricePool.length + (hasCustomPrice ? 1 : 0);\n  // For custom price: is it strictly the cheapest? (would dethrone min)\n  const customBeatsMin = hasCustomPrice && validPricePool.length > 0 && priceUnderEval < minPrice;\n  const savingsVsMin   = hasCustomPrice ? Math.max(0, minPrice - priceUnderEval) : 0;\n  const overhangVsAvg  = hasCustomPrice && avgPrice > 0 ? Math.round(priceUnderEval - avgPrice) : 0;\n\n  /* TierTabs — switchable 3-tier comparison selector.\n     `dark` swaps the palette for the dark-themed footer header. */\n  const renderTierTabs = (dark: boolean) => (\n    <div style={{\n      display: \"inline-flex\", gap: \"2px\",\n      background: dark ? \"rgba(255,255,255,0.06)\" : \"#f5f0e8\",\n      borderRadius: \"7px\", padding: \"2px\", flexShrink: 0,\n    }}>\n      {([\"exact\", \"similar\", \"broad\"] as Tier[]).map((t) => {\n        const meta     = TIER_META[t];\n        const isActive = tier === t;\n        const count    = tierPools[t].length;\n        const disabled = count === 0;\n        const activeColor = (isActive && isHighDeviation) ? \"#e74c3c\" : meta.color;\n        return (\n          <button\n            key={t}\n            disabled={disabled}\n            onClick={() => {\n              setUserTier(t);\n              // Reset stat-cell cycle indices so the new tier starts fresh\n              setMinCycleIdx(0);\n              setAvgCycleIdx(0);\n              setMaxCycleIdx(0);\n            }}\n            title={`${meta.tip}${disabled ? \" — لا توجد بنود\" : \"\"}`}\n            style={{\n              display: \"inline-flex\", alignItems: \"center\", gap: \"4px\",\n              fontSize: \"0.58rem\", fontWeight: 700,\n              padding: \"3px 8px\", borderRadius: \"5px\", border: \"none\",\n              cursor: disabled ? \"not-allowed\" : \"pointer\",\n              background: isActive ? activeColor : \"transparent\",\n              color: isActive ? \"#fff\" : (dark ? \"rgba(255,255,255,0.55)\" : \"#888\"),\n              opacity: disabled ? 0.35 : 1,\n              transition: \"all 0.18s\",\n              fontFamily: \"inherit\",\n              whiteSpace: \"nowrap\",\n            }}\n          >\n            <span style={{ fontSize: \"0.62rem\", lineHeight: 1 }}>{meta.icon}</span>\n            {meta.label}\n            <span style={{\n              background: isActive ? \"rgba(255,255,255,0.28)\" : (dark ? \"rgba(255,255,255,0.10)\" : \"#e8e0d0\"),\n              borderRadius: \"3px\", padding: \"0 4px\", fontWeight: 800,\n              fontSize: \"0.54rem\", minWidth: \"14px\", textAlign: \"center\",\n            }}>{count}</span>\n          </button>\n        );\n      })}\n    </div>\n  );\n\n  /* MaskRibbon — shows the matching prefix for the active tier, with\n     trailing underscores for the \"free\" digits.  Helps the user see\n     exactly which parts of the code drove the comparison. */\n  const renderMaskRibbon = (dark: boolean) => (\n    <span\n      title={`القناع المُستخدم في المقارنة — الخانات الثابتة ظاهرة بالأرقام والخانات الحرة بـ _`}\n      style={{\n        fontFamily: \"monospace\", fontSize: \"0.58rem\", fontWeight: 700,\n        letterSpacing: \"0.06em\",\n        color: dark ? \"rgba(255,255,255,0.85)\" : \"var(--charcoal)\",\n        background: dark ? \"rgba(197,160,89,0.18)\" : \"rgba(197,160,89,0.12)\",\n        border: `1px solid ${dark ? \"rgba(197,160,89,0.35)\" : \"rgba(197,160,89,0.30)\"}`,\n        borderRadius: \"4px\", padding: \"2px 7px\",\n        whiteSpace: \"nowrap\", flexShrink: 0,\n        direction: \"ltr\",\n      }}\n    >{tierMask}</span>\n  );\n\n  /* Deviation warning chip — only shown when |evaluated − avg| / avg > 30%.\n     The label adapts to whichever price is under evaluation. */\n  const renderDeviationChip = () => isHighDeviation ? (\n    <span\n      title={`${evalLabel} (${formatExact(priceUnderEval)}) ينحرف بنسبة ${(deviationPct * 100).toFixed(0)}٪ عن متوسط هذا المستوى (${formatExact(Math.round(avgPrice))})`}\n      style={{\n        display: \"inline-flex\", alignItems: \"center\", gap: \"3px\",\n        fontSize: \"0.55rem\", fontWeight: 800, color: \"#fff\",\n        background: \"#e74c3c\", borderRadius: \"4px\", padding: \"2px 6px\",\n        whiteSpace: \"nowrap\", flexShrink: 0,\n        animation: \"pulse-gold 1.5s ease-in-out infinite\",\n      }}\n    >🔴 {hasCustomPrice ? \"السعر المُدخل\" : \"انحراف\"} {(deviationPct * 100).toFixed(0)}٪</span>\n  ) : null;\n\n  /* Rank chip — shows where the evaluated price would sit in the tier pool.\n     Always visible when there is something to compare against (≥2 records).\n     For custom price the chip is purple (to match the existing \"السعر المقارن\" cell color). */\n  const renderRankChip = (dark: boolean) => {\n    if (validPricePool.length < 2 || priceUnderEval <= 0) return null;\n    const color   = hasCustomPrice ? \"#9b59b6\" : \"#c5a059\";\n    const isBest  = evalRank === 1;\n    const icon    = isBest ? \"🏆\" : hasCustomPrice ? \"💡\" : \"📊\";\n    return (\n      <span\n        title={`${evalLabel} (${formatExact(priceUnderEval)}) يحتل الترتيب ${evalRank} من ${evalTotal} في هذا المستوى`}\n        style={{\n          display: \"inline-flex\", alignItems: \"center\", gap: \"3px\",\n          fontSize: \"0.55rem\", fontWeight: 800,\n          color: isBest ? \"#fff\" : color,\n          background: isBest ? color : (dark ? `${color}22` : `${color}14`),\n          border: `1px solid ${color}${dark ? \"55\" : \"40\"}`,\n          borderRadius: \"4px\", padding: \"2px 6px\",\n          whiteSpace: \"nowrap\", flexShrink: 0, direction: \"rtl\",\n        }}\n      >{icon} الترتيب {evalRank}/{evalTotal}</span>\n    );\n  };\n\n  // ── Strict tertile pools — NO price value appears in more than one pool ──\n  // Sort all by price then slice into three equal (±1) groups.\n  // Boundary adjustment: when duplicate prices straddle the cut point, the\n  // entire group is moved to keep pools price-disjoint:\n  //   • maxStart walks backward until _allSorted[maxStart-1].price differs\n  //   • minEnd walks forward until _allSorted[minEnd].price differs\n  // Edge cases: n≤1 → all pools same record; n=2 → min=[0], avg=[], max=[1].\n  const _allSorted = [...validPricePool].sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price);\n  const _n = _allSorted.length;\n  const _third = Math.floor(_n / 3);\n\n  let minPool: typeof _allSorted;\n  let avgPool: typeof _allSorted;\n  let maxPool: typeof _allSorted;\n\n  if (_n <= 1) {\n    minPool = _allSorted; maxPool = _allSorted; avgPool = [];\n  } else if (_n === 2) {\n    minPool = [_allSorted[0]]; maxPool = [_allSorted[1]]; avgPool = [];\n  } else {\n    let minEnd   = _third || 1;\n    let maxStart = _n - (_third || 1);\n\n    // Pull maxStart backward to absorb all records sharing the boundary price\n    const maxBoundaryPrice = _allSorted[maxStart].price;\n    while (maxStart > minEnd && _allSorted[maxStart - 1].price === maxBoundaryPrice) {\n      maxStart--;\n    }\n\n    // Push minEnd forward to absorb all records sharing the boundary price\n    const minBoundaryPrice = _allSorted[minEnd - 1].price;\n    while (minEnd < maxStart && _allSorted[minEnd].price === minBoundaryPrice) {\n      minEnd++;\n    }\n\n    minPool = _allSorted.slice(0, minEnd);\n    maxPool = [..._allSorted.slice(maxStart)].reverse();\n    avgPool = [..._allSorted.slice(minEnd, maxStart)].sort(\n      (a, b) => Math.abs(a.price - avgPrice) - Math.abs(b.price - avgPrice)\n    );\n  }\n\n  // Show avg cell only when its pool is non-empty\n  const hasMidContractor = avgPool.length > 0;\n\n  // Current cycle positions — each pool wraps independently\n  const contractorWithMin    = minPool[minCycleIdx % Math.max(1, minPool.length)]  ?? minPool[0];\n  const contractorWithMax    = maxPool[maxCycleIdx % Math.max(1, maxPool.length)]  ?? maxPool[0];\n  const contractorAtAvgCycle = avgPool.length > 0\n    ? avgPool[avgCycleIdx % avgPool.length]\n    : undefined;\n\n  // ── Best 5: Best Value scoring = 60% price competitiveness + 40% rating ──\n  // A contractor with a high rating and a competitive price ranks above one that\n  // is cheapest but has a low rating (Best Value = Quality × Price together).\n  const _maxPoolPrice = maxPrice > 0 ? maxPrice : 1;\n  const best5 = validPricePool.length > 0\n    ? [...validPricePool]\n        .map((c) => {\n          const rating = Math.max(0, Math.min(5, Number((c as any).rating ?? 0)));\n          const normalizedRating       = rating / 5;\n          const normalizedPriceScore   = 1 - (c.price / _maxPoolPrice); // lower price → higher score\n          const bestValueScore         = normalizedRating * 0.4 + normalizedPriceScore * 0.6;\n          return { ...c, _bestValueScore: bestValueScore };\n        })\n        .sort((a, b) => b._bestValueScore - a._bestValueScore)\n        .slice(0, 5)\n    : [];\n\n  // ── Work history: same contractor + same item tier (mirrors comparison pool) ──\n  // When the current record has an itemCode we match by code prefix — the same\n  // tier logic used by the price-comparison chart — so only bids on the same\n  // (or similar) item family are shown, preventing unrelated work types from\n  // bleeding in.  When there is no itemCode (legacy data) we fall back to\n  // workType matching, identical to the legacy comparison fallback above.\n  const contractorNameKey = contractor ? normalize(contractor.contractor) : \"\";\n  const workHistory: Contractor[] = contractor && contractorNameKey.length > 0\n    ? (() => {\n        const sameContractor = (c: Contractor) =>\n          c.id !== contractor.id && normalize(c.contractor) === contractorNameKey;\n\n        if (hasCode) {\n          // Similar tier — same first 5 code slots (portfolio-independent)\n          if (digitsPrefix5) {\n            const similar = allContractors.filter((c) => {\n              if (!sameContractor(c)) return false;\n              const d = codeDigits((c as any).itemCode);\n              return !!d && d.startsWith(digitsPrefix5);\n            });\n            if (similar.length > 0) return similar.slice(0, 50);\n          }\n          // Broad tier — same first 3 code slots (portfolio-independent)\n          if (digitsPrefix3) {\n            const broad = allContractors.filter((c) => {\n              if (!sameContractor(c)) return false;\n              const d = codeDigits((c as any).itemCode);\n              return !!d && d.startsWith(digitsPrefix3);\n            });\n            if (broad.length > 0) return broad.slice(0, 50);\n          }\n        }\n\n        // Legacy fallback — no itemCode on current record (or no prefix match found)\n        const workTypeKey = normalize(contractor.workType ?? \"\");\n        return allContractors\n          .filter((c) => sameContractor(c) && normalize(c.workType) === workTypeKey)\n          .slice(0, 50);\n      })()\n    : [];\n\n  if (!contractor) {\n    return (\n      <main className=\"content-area\">\n        <div className=\"card animate-fade-up\" style={{ textAlign: \"center\", padding: \"50px 24px\" }}>\n          <Building2 size={52} style={{ color: \"#ddd\", margin: \"0 auto 14px\" }} />\n          <p style={{ color: \"#bbb\", fontSize: \"0.9rem\" }}>\n            {emptyStateMessage ?? \"اختر مقاولاً من القائمة الجانبية أو استخدم البحث الشامل\"}\n          </p>\n        </div>\n      </main>\n    );\n  }\n\n  const rating       = (contractor as any).rating as number | null | undefined;\n  const localContent = (contractor as any).localContent as string | null | undefined;\n\n  // ── Footer stats array — shared by grid cells AND comparison bar ──\n  const footerStats: Array<{\n    label: string; sub2: string; value: string; color: string;\n    id: number | null; rawPrice: number; isCustom?: boolean; isBest?: boolean;\n    cycleCount?: number; cyclePos?: number;\n  }> = [\n    customPrice && customPrice > 0\n      ? { label: \"السعر المقارن\", sub2: \"مقاول خارج القاعدة\", value: formatExact(customPrice), color: \"#9b59b6\", id: null, isCustom: true, rawPrice: customPrice }\n      : { label: \"سعر المقاول الحالي\", sub2: contractor.contractor ?? \"—\", value: formatExact(contractor.price), color: \"var(--gold)\", id: contractor.id as number | null, isCustom: false, rawPrice: contractor.price },\n    {\n      label: \"أدنى سعر لهذا البند\",\n      sub2: minPool.length > 1\n        ? `${contractorWithMin?.contractor ?? \"—\"} (${minCycleIdx % minPool.length + 1}/${minPool.length})`\n        : contractorWithMin?.contractor ?? \"—\",\n      value: formatExact(contractorWithMin?.price ?? minPrice), color: \"#2baa74\",\n      id: contractorWithMin?.id ?? null, isBest: contractor.price === minPrice, rawPrice: contractorWithMin?.price ?? minPrice,\n      cycleCount: minPool.length, cyclePos: minCycleIdx,\n    },\n    // Show avg only when the middle tertile pool is non-empty (≥3 records).\n    hasMidContractor\n      ? {\n          label: \"متوسط الأسعار لهذا البند\",\n          sub2: avgPool.length > 1\n            ? `${contractorAtAvgCycle?.contractor ?? \"—\"} (${avgCycleIdx % avgPool.length + 1}/${avgPool.length})`\n            : contractorAtAvgCycle?.contractor ?? \"—\",\n          value: formatExact(contractorAtAvgCycle?.price ?? avgPrice),\n          color: \"#3b8fcc\",\n          id: contractorAtAvgCycle?.id ?? null,\n          rawPrice: contractorAtAvgCycle?.price ?? avgPrice,\n          cycleCount: avgPool.length, cyclePos: avgCycleIdx,\n        }\n      : {\n          label: \"متوسط الأسعار لهذا البند\",\n          sub2: \"لا يوجد سعر متوسط\",\n          value: \"—\",\n          color: \"#3b8fcc\",\n          id: null,\n          rawPrice: 0,\n        },\n    {\n      label: \"أعلى سعر لهذا البند\",\n      sub2: maxPool.length > 1\n        ? `${contractorWithMax?.contractor ?? \"—\"} (${maxCycleIdx % maxPool.length + 1}/${maxPool.length})`\n        : contractorWithMax?.contractor ?? \"—\",\n      value: formatExact(contractorWithMax?.price ?? maxPrice), color: \"#e74c3c\",\n      id: contractorWithMax?.id ?? null, rawPrice: contractorWithMax?.price ?? maxPrice,\n      cycleCount: maxPool.length, cyclePos: maxCycleIdx,\n    },\n  ];\n  // النشاط الرئيسي: يُعطى الأولوية لقيمة السجل الحالي، وإذا كانت فارغة\n  // نبحث عن أي سجل آخر لنفس المقاول يحتوي على النشاط الرئيسي.\n  const rawMainActivity = (contractor as any).mainActivity as string | null | undefined;\n  const mainActivity: string | null | undefined = rawMainActivity || (() => {\n    const cName = normalize(contractor.contractor);\n    const found = allContractors.find(\n      (c) => normalize(c.contractor) === cName && !!(c as any).mainActivity\n    );\n    return found ? ((found as any).mainActivity as string) : undefined;\n  })();\n\n  return (\n    <main className=\"content-area\">\n\n      {/* ── 1. بطاقة بيانات المقاول ── */}\n      <div className=\"card animate-fade-up\" style={{ marginBottom: \"16px\", padding: 0, overflow: \"hidden\" }}>\n        <div style={{ background: \"linear-gradient(135deg, var(--charcoal) 0%, #2d2420 100%)\", padding: \"16px 20px\", display: \"flex\", justifyContent: \"space-between\", alignItems: \"flex-start\", gap: \"12px\" }}>\n          <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>\n            <div style={{ fontSize: \"0.58rem\", color: \"rgba(197,160,89,0.65)\", textTransform: \"uppercase\", letterSpacing: \"0.1em\", marginBottom: \"5px\" }}>\n              بيانات المقاول الرئيسية\n            </div>\n            {/* Contractor name */}\n            <h2 style={{ fontSize: \"0.98rem\", fontWeight: 800, color: \"#ffffff\", lineHeight: 1.3, margin: \"0 0 5px 0\" }}>\n              {contractor.contractor}\n            </h2>\n            {/* Contract number + contract year side by side */}\n            <div style={{ display: \"flex\", alignItems: \"center\", gap: \"8px\" }}>\n              <div style={{ fontSize: \"0.6rem\", color: \"rgba(255,255,255,0.35)\", letterSpacing: \"0.04em\" }}>\n                {contractor.contractNo}\n              </div>\n              {contractor.contractYear && (\n                <div style={{ fontSize: \"0.58rem\", color: \"rgba(197,160,89,0.6)\", background: \"rgba(197,160,89,0.1)\", borderRadius: \"4px\", padding: \"1px 7px\", letterSpacing: \"0.04em\", fontWeight: 700 }}>\n                  {contractor.contractYear}\n                </div>\n              )}\n            </div>\n          </div>\n          <div style={{ textAlign: \"left\", flexShrink: 0, display: \"flex\", flexDirection: \"column\", alignItems: \"flex-end\" }}>\n            <div style={{ fontSize: \"0.55rem\", color: \"rgba(255,255,255,0.38)\", textTransform: \"uppercase\", letterSpacing: \"0.08em\" }}>سعر البند</div>\n            <div style={{ fontSize: \"1.2rem\", fontWeight: 900, color: \"var(--gold)\", lineHeight: 1, direction: \"ltr\" }}>\n              {formatExact(contractor.price)}\n            </div>\n            <div style={{ fontSize: \"0.55rem\", color: \"rgba(255,255,255,0.35)\", marginBottom: \"6px\" }}>ريال سعودي</div>\n            {/* Stars under price, bottom-left of price column */}\n            <StarInline rating={rating} />\n          </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <div style={{ display: \"grid\", gridTemplateColumns: \"repeat(3, 1fr)\", borderBottom: \"1px solid #f0ebe0\" }}>\n          {[\n            { icon: <MapPin size={12} />,    label: \"المحفظة\",        value: contractor.portfolio },\n            { icon: <Building2 size={12} />, label: \"المشروع\",        value: contractor.project },\n            { icon: <Briefcase size={12} />, label: \"النشاط الرئيسي\", value: mainActivity || \"—\" },\n          ].map((item, i) => (\n            <div\n              key={i}\n              style={{ padding: \"12px 16px\", borderLeft: i < 2 ? \"1px solid #f0ebe0\" : \"none\", transition: \"background 0.18s\" }}\n              onMouseEnter={(e) => (e.currentTarget.style.background = \"rgba(197,160,89,0.04)\")}\n              onMouseLeave={(e) => (e.currentTarget.style.background = \"\")}\n            >\n              <div style={{ display: \"flex\", alignItems: \"center\", gap: \"5px\", marginBottom: \"3px\" }}>\n                <span style={{ color: \"var(--gold)\" }}>{item.icon}</span>\n                <span style={{ fontSize: \"0.55rem\", color: \"#bbb\", textTransform: \"uppercase\", letterSpacing: \"0.06em\" }}>{item.label}</span>\n              </div>\n              <div style={{ fontSize: \"0.78rem\", fontWeight: 700, color: \"var(--charcoal)\" }}>{item.value}</div>\n            </div>\n          ))}\n        </div>\n\n        {/* Contact + Local Content row */}\n        <div style={{ display: \"grid\", gridTemplateColumns: \"1fr 1fr 1fr\", background: \"#faf8f4\" }}>\n          {[\n            { icon: <Phone size={11} />, label: \"رقم التواصل\",       value: contractor.phone },\n            { icon: <Mail size={11} />,  label: \"البريد الإلكتروني\", value: contractor.email },\n            {\n              icon: <span style={{ fontSize: \"11px\", fontWeight: 800, color: \"var(--gold)\" }}>🏭</span>,\n              label: \"المحتوى المحلي\",\n              value: localContent || \"—\",\n            },\n          ].map((item, i) => (\n            <div key={i} style={{ padding: \"10px 16px\", display: \"flex\", alignItems: \"center\", gap: \"7px\", borderLeft: i < 2 ? \"1px solid #f0ebe0\" : \"none\" }}>\n              <span style={{ color: \"var(--gold)\", flexShrink: 0 }}>{item.icon}</span>\n              <div style={{ minWidth: 0 }}>\n                <div style={{ fontSize: \"0.55rem\", color: \"#ccc\", textTransform: \"uppercase\", letterSpacing: \"0.05em\" }}>{item.label}</div>\n                <div style={{ fontSize: \"0.76rem\", fontWeight: 600, color: \"var(--charcoal)\", overflow: \"hidden\", textOverflow: \"ellipsis\", whiteSpace: \"nowrap\" }}>{item.value}</div>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n          ))}\n        </div>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* ── 2. نطاق التوصيف الفني للبند ── */}\n      <div className=\"card animate-fade-up\" style={{ marginBottom: \"16px\", animationDelay: \"0.05s\" }}>\n        <div style={{ display: \"flex\", alignItems: \"center\", gap: \"10px\", marginBottom: \"14px\", paddingBottom: \"10px\", borderBottom: \"2px solid rgba(197,160,89,0.12)\" }}>\n          <div style={{ width: \"32px\", height: \"32px\", borderRadius: \"8px\", background: \"linear-gradient(135deg, var(--gold), أقل من ${refLabel} بـ ${formatExact(diff)} ر.س (${pct}%)`;\n            return (\n              <div style={{ padding: \"8px 16px\", borderTop: `1px solid ${noteColor}55`, background: }}>{text}</span>\n              </div>\n            );\n          })()}\n\n          {/* Saving indicator — only shown when current contractor IS the lowest in the pool */}\n          {!customPrice && containsMatch(c.measurements       ?? \"\",  search) ||\n        containsMatch(c.itemCode           ?? \"\",  search) ||\n        containsMatch(c.workCategory       ?? \"\",  search) ||\n        containsMatch(c.unit               ?? \"\",  search) ||\n        containsMatch(c.phone,                     search) ||\n        containsMatch(c.email,                     search) ||\n
