\"./filterTypes\";\nimport { EMPTY_FILTERS } from \"./filterTypes\";\n\ninterface FilterBarProps {\n  filters:         FilterState;\n  onFiltersChange: (f: FilterState) => void;\n  search?:         string;\n}\n\n/* ── Arabic normalizer for in-dropdown search ── */\nfunction normalize(s: string) {\n  return (s ?? \"\")\n    .replace(/[\\u064B-\\u065F]/g, \"\")\n    .replace(/[أإآ]/g, \"ا\")\n    .replace(/ة/g, \"ه\")\n    .replace(/ى/g, \"ي\")\n    .toLowerCase()\n    .trim();\n}\n\n/* ── Extract unique, sorted, non-empty values from a field ── */\nfunction getUnique(contractors: Contractor[], getter: (c: Contractor) => string): string[] {\n  const seen = new Set<string>();\n  const result: string[] = [];\n  for (const c of contractors) {\n    const val = (getter(c) ?? \"\").trim();\n    if (val && !seen.has(val)) {\n      seen.add(val);\n      result.push(val);\n    }\n  }\n  return result.sort((a, b) => a.localeCompare(b, \"ar\"));\n}\n\n/* ── Exact-match (for filter pills) ── */\nfunction strictMatch(haystack: string, needle: string): boolean {\n  if (!needle) return true;\n  return normalize(haystack) === normalize(needle);\n}\n\n/* ── Contains-match (for the global search bar) ── */\nfunction matchesSearch(c: Contractor, q: string): boolean {\n  if (!q) return true;\n  const n = normalize(q);\n  return [\n    c.contractNo, c.contractor, c.project, c.portfolio,\n    c.workType, c.technicalScope,\n    c.businessProgram  ?? \"\",\n    c.workFamily       ?? \"\",\n    c.workCategory     ?? \"\",\n    c.mainActivity     ?? \"\",\n    c.itemScope        ?? \"\",\n    c.techSpecs        ?? \"\",\n    c.measurements     ?? \"\",\n    c.unit             ?? \"\",\n    String(c.price ?? \"\"),\n    c.phone ?? \"\", c.email ?? \"\",\n  ].some((field) => normalize(String(field)).includes(n));\n}\n\n/* ── Filter → DB column mapping ── */\nconst FILTER_DEFS: {\n  key:    keyof FilterState;\n  label:  string;\n  getter: (c: Contractor) => string;\n}[] = [\n  { key: \"portfolio\",       label: \"المحفظة\",            getter: (c) => c.portfolio },\n  { key: \"mainActivity\",    label: \"النشاط الرئيسي\",     getter: (c) => c.mainActivity     ?? \"\" },\n  { key: \"businessProgram\", label: \"برنامج الأعمال\",     getter: (c) => c.businessProgram  ?? \"\" },\n  { key: \"workFamily\",      label: \"عائلة الأعمال\",      getter: (c) => c.workFamily       ?? \"\" },\n  { key: \"workType\",        label: \"نوع الأعمال\",        getter: (c) => c.workType },\n  { key: \"itemScope\",       label: \"شمولية البند\",       getter: (c) => c.itemScope        ?? \"\" },\n  { key: \"techSpecs\",       label: \"مواصفات فنية\",       getter: (c) => c.techSpecs        ?? \"\" },\n  { key: \"measurements\",    label: \"قياسات\",             getter: (c) => c.measurements     ?? \"\" },\n  { key: \"workCategory\",    label: \"نوع التعاقد\",        getter: (c) => c.workCategory     ?? \"\" },\n];\n\n/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n   Single dropdown — portal-based so it escapes any overflow /\n   stacking-context boundary inside the header.\n   ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */\nfunction FilterDropdown({\n  label,\n  value,\n  allOptions,\n  onSelect,\n  onClear,\n}: {\n  label:      string;\n  value:      string;\n  allOptions: string[];   // full list; computed lazily by parent when open\n  onSelect:   (v: string) => void;\n  onClear:    () => void;\n}) {\n  const [open, setOpen]               = useState(false);\n  const [innerSearch, setInnerSearch] = useState(\"\");\n  const [rect, setRect]               = useState<DOMRect | null>(null);\n\n  const triggerRef   = useRef<HTMLButtonElement>(null);\n  const searchRef    = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);\n  const panelRef     = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);\n\n  const isActive = value !== \"\";\n\n  /* Measure trigger position whenever the dropdown opens */\n  function openDropdown() {\n    if (triggerRef.current) {\n      setRect(triggerRef.current.getBoundingClientRect());\n    }\n    setOpen(true);\n    setInnerSearch(\"\");\n  }\n\n  /* Close on outside click (anywhere in document) */\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!open) return;\n    function onDown(e: MouseEvent) {\n      if (\n        triggerRef.current?.contains(e.target as Node) ||\n        panelRef.current?.contains(e.target as Node)\n      ) return;\n      setOpen(false);\n      setInnerSearch(\"\");\n    }\n    document.addEventListener(\"mousedown\", onDown);\n    return () => document.removeEventListener(\"mousedown\", onDown);\n  }, [open]);\n\n  /* Close on scroll / resize so portal position stays consistent */\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!open) return;\n    const close = () => { setOpen(false); setInnerSearch(\"\"); };\n    window.addEventListener(\"scroll\", close, { passive: true });\n    window.addEventListener(\"resize\", close, { passive: true });\n    return () => {\n      window.removeEventListener(\"scroll\", close);\n      window.removeEventListener(\"resize\", close);\n    };\n  }, [open]);\n\n  /* Auto-focus inner search when panel mounts */\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (open) setTimeout(() => searchRef.current?.focus(), 60);\n  }, [open]);\n\n  /* Portal panel position: anchored below the trigger button */\n  const panelStyle: React.CSSProperties = rect\n    ? {\n        position:  \"fixed\",\n        top:       rect.bottom + 8,\n        right:     window.innerWidth - rect.right,\n        width:     \"max-content\",\n        minWidth:  Math.max(rect.width, 210),\n        maxWidth:  340,\n        zIndex:    9999,\n      }\n    : { display: \"none\" };\n\n  /* Options filtered by the in-dropdown search */\n  const filteredOpts = useMemo(\n    () => allOptions.filter((o) => normalize(o).includes(normalize(innerSearch))),\n    [allOptions, innerSearch],\n  );\n\n  function handleSelect(v: string) {\n    onSelect(v);\n    setOpen(false);\n    setInnerSearch(\"\");\n  }\n\n  /* ── Trigger pill ── */\n  const pillStyle: React.CSSProperties = {\n    display:        \"flex\",\n    alignItems:     \"center\",\n    gap:            \"4px\",\n    padding:        \"4px 9px\",\n    borderRadius:   \"20px\",\n    border:         isActive ? \"1.5px solid var(--gold)\" : \"1.5px solid rgba(197,160,89,0.30)\",\n    background:     isActive ? \"rgba(197,160,89,0.18)\" : \"rgba(255,255,255,0.08)\",\n    color:          isActive ? \"var(--gold)\" : \"rgba(255,255,255,0.80)\",\n    fontSize:       \"0.63rem\",\n    fontWeight:     isActive ? 700 : 500,\n    fontFamily:     \"Tajawal, sans-serif\",\n    cursor:         \"pointer\",\n    whiteSpace:     \"nowrap\",\n    backdropFilter: \"blur(8px)\",\n    boxShadow:      isActive ? \"0 0 12px rgba(197,160,89,0.22)\" : \"none\",\n    letterSpacing:  \"0.01em\",\n    transition:     \"all 0.18s\",\n    flexShrink:     0,\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div style={{ position: \"relative\", flexShrink: 0 }}>\n      {/* ── Trigger ── */}\n      <button\n        ref={triggerRef}\n        onClick={() => (open ? (setOpen(false), setInnerSearch(\"\")) : openDropdown())}\n        style={pillStyle}\n        onMouseEnter={(e) => {\n          if (!isActive) {\n            const b = e.currentTarget;\n            b.style.borderColor = \"rgba(197,160,89,0.55)\";\n            b.style.background  = \"rgba(255,255,255,0.13)\";\n            b.style.color       = \"#fff\";\n          }\n        }}\n        onMouseLeave={(e) => {\n          if (!isActive) {\n            const b = e.currentTarget;\n            b.style.borderColor = \"rgba(197,160,89,0.30)\";\n            b.style.background  = \"rgba(255,255,255,0.08)\";\n            b.style.color       = \"rgba(255,255,255,0.80)\";\n          }\n        }}\n      >\n        <span style={{ maxWidth: \"130px\", overflow: \"hidden\", textOverflow: \"ellipsis\" }}>\n          {isActive ? value : label}\n        </span>\n\n        {isActive ? (\n          <span\n            onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); onClear(); setOpen(false); }}\n            style={{\n              display: \"inline-flex\", alignItems: \"center\", justifyContent: \"center\",\n              width: \"16px\", height: \"16px\", borderRadius: \"50%\",\n              background: \"rgba(197,160,89,0.35)\", color: \"var(--gold)\",\n              cursor: \"pointer\", flexShrink: 0, transition: \"background 0.15s\",\n            }}\n            onMouseEnter={(e) => ((e.currentTarget as HTMLElement).style.background = \"rgba(197,160,89,0.6)\")}\n            onMouseLeave={(e) => ((e.currentTarget as HTMLElement).style.background = \"rgba(197,160,89,0.35)\")}\n          >\n            <X size={9} />\n          </span>\n        ) : (\n          <ChevronDown\n            size={12}\n            style={{\n              transition: \"transform 0.18s\",\n              transform:  open ? \"rotate(180deg)\" : \"rotate(0deg)\",\n              flexShrink: 0,\n            }}\n          />\n        )}\n      </button>\n\n      {/* ── Portal Panel — renders at <body> to escape all overflow contexts ── */}\n      {open && createPortal(\n        <div\n          ref={panelRef}\n          style={{\n            ...panelStyle,\n            background:     \"rgba(250,246,240,0.98)\",\n            border:         \"1.5px solid rgba(197,160,89,0.35)\",\n            borderRadius:   \"13px\",\n            boxShadow:      \"0 8px 32px rgba(58,54,50,0.15)\",\n            overflow:       \"hidden\",\n            backdropFilter: \"blur(16px)\",\n            animation:      \"filterDropIn 0.15s ease\",\n            boxSizing:      \"border-box\" as const,\n          }}\n        >\n          {/* ── Inner search ── */}\n          <div style={{ padding: \"10px 10px 8px\", borderBottom: \"1px solid rgba(197,160,89,0.15)\", background: \"rgba(197,160,89,0.05)\" }}>\n            <input\n              ref={searchRef}\n              type=\"text\"\n              placeholder={`بحث في ${label}...`}\n              value={innerSearch}\n              onChange={(e) => setInnerSearch(e.target.value)}\n              style={{\n                width: \"100%\", padding: \"7px 11px\",\n                background: \"rgba(255,255,255,0.70)\",\n                border: \"1px solid rgba(197,160,89,0.30)\",\n                borderRadius: \"8px\",\n                fontSize: \"0.72rem\", fontFamily: \"Tajawal, sans-serif\",\n                direction: \"rtl\", color: \"#3a3632\", outline: \"none\",\n                boxSizing: \"border-box\", transition: \"border-color 0.18s\",\n              }}\n              onFocus={(e) => (e.target.style.borderColor = \"rgba(197,160,89,0.75)\")}\n              onBlur={(e)  => (e.target.style.borderColor = \"rgba(197,160,89,0.30)\")}\n            />\n          </div>\n\n          {/* ── Scrollable options ── */}\n          <div className=\"dark-scroll\" style={{ maxHeight: \"260px\", overflowY: \"auto\" }}>\n            {filteredOpts.length === 0 ? (\n              <div style={{ padding: \"18px 14px\", textAlign: \"center\", fontSize: \"0.72rem\", color: \"rgba(58,54,50,0.40)\", fontFamily: \"Tajawal, sans-serif\" }}>\n                لا توجد نتائج مطابقة\n              </div>\n            ) : filteredOpts.map((opt) => {\n              const sel = opt === value;\n              return (\n                <div\n                  key={opt}\n                  onClick={() => handleSelect(opt)}\n                  style={{\n                    padding: \"9px 14px\", fontSize: \"0.75rem\",\n                    fontFamily: \"Tajawal, sans-serif\", direction: \"rtl\",\n                    cursor: \"pointer\",\n                    color:       sel ? \"#a88540\" : \"rgba(58,54,50,0.85)\",\n                    background:  sel ? \"rgba(197,160,89,0.12)\" : \"transparent\",\n                    fontWeight:  sel ? 700 : 400,\n                    borderRight: sel ? \"3px solid var(--gold)\" : \"3px solid transparent\",\n                    transition:  \"background 0.12s, color 0.12s\",\n                    display: \"flex\", alignItems: \"center\", justifyContent: \"space-between\", gap: \"12px\",\n                    whiteSpace: \"nowrap\",\n                  }}\n                  onMouseEnter={(e) => {\n                    if (!sel) {\n                      (e.currentTarget as HTMLDivElement).style.background = \"rgba(197,160,89,0.10)\";\n                      (e.currentTarget as HTMLDivElement).style.color      = \"#3a3632\";\n                    }\n                  }}\n                  onMouseLeave={(e) => {\n                    if (!sel) {\n                      (e.currentTarget as HTMLDivElement).style.background = \"transparent\";\n                      (e.currentTarget as HTMLDivElement).style.color      = \"rgba(58,54,50,0.85)\";\n                    }\n                  }}\n                >\n                  <span>{opt}</span>\n                  {sel && <span style={{ fontSize: \"0.65rem\", color: \"var(--gold)\", flexShrink: 0 }}>✓</span>}\n                </div>\n              );\n            })}\n          </div>\n\n          {/* ── Footer count ── */}\n          <div style={{ padding: \"5px 14px\", borderTop: \"1px solid rgba(197,160,89,0.15)\", fontSize: \"0.6rem\", color: \"rgba(58,54,50,0.40)\", textAlign: \"center\", fontFamily: \"Tajawal, sans-serif\" }}>\n            {filteredOpts.length} خيار متاح\n          </div>\n        </div>,\n        document.body,\n      )}\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n\n/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n   PriceInputPill — inline number entry in the same pill row\n   ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */\nfunction PriceInputPill({\n  value,\n  onChange,\n  onClear,\n  disabled,\n}: {\n  value:    string;\n  onChange: (v: string) => void;\n  onClear:  () => void;\n  disabled: boolean;\n}) {\n  const isActive = !disabled && value.trim() !== \"\";\n\n  const pillStyle: React.CSSProperties = {\n    display:        \"flex\",\n    alignItems:     \"center\",\n    gap:            \"4px\",\n    padding:        \"2px 7px 2px 8px\",\n    borderRadius:   \"20px\",\n    border:         disabled\n      ? \"1.5px solid rgba(197,160,89,0.12)\"\n      : isActive ? \"1.5px solid var(--gold)\" : \"1.5px solid rgba(197,160,89,0.30)\",\n    background:     disabled\n      ? \"rgba(255,255,255,0.03)\"\n      : isActive ? \"rgba(197,160,89,0.18)\" : \"rgba(255,255,255,0.08)\",\n    backdropFilter: \"blur(8px)\",\n    boxShadow:      isActive ? \"0 0 12px rgba(197,160,89,0.22)\" : \"none\",\n    transition:     \"all 0.18s\",\n    flexShrink:     0,\n    whiteSpace:     \"nowrap\",\n    opacity:        disabled ? 0.38 : 1,\n    cursor:         disabled ? \"not-allowed\" : \"default\",\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div style={pillStyle} title={disabled ? \"يُفعَّل عند كتابة نص في البحث أو تحديد فلتر آخر\" : undefined}>\n      <span style={{ fontSize: \"0.57rem\", color: isActive ? \"var(--gold)\" : \"rgba(255,255,255,0.55)\", fontWeight: 600, fontFamily: \"Tajawal, sans-serif\", flexShrink: 0 }}>\n        سعر البند\n      </span>\n      <input\n        type=\"number\"\n        min={0}\n        placeholder=\"0\"\n        value={value}\n        disabled={disabled}\n        onChange={(e) => !disabled && onChange(e.target.value)}\n        className=\"price-no-spin\"\n        style={{\n          width:       \"40px\",\n          background:  \"transparent\",\n          border:      \"none\",\n          outline:     \"none\",\n          fontSize:    \"0.57rem\",\n          fontWeight:  isActive ? 700 : 400,\n          color:       isActive ? \"var(--gold)\" : \"rgba(255,255,255,0.45)\",\n          fontFamily:  \"Tajawal, sans-serif\",\n          direction:   \"ltr\",\n          textAlign:   \"right\",\n          cursor:      disabled ? \"not-allowed\" : \"text\",\n        }}\n        onFocus={(e) => {\n          if (disabled) return;\n          (e.currentTarget.parentElement as HTMLDivElement).style.borderColor = \"rgba(197,160,89,0.75)\";\n          (e.currentTarget.parentElement as HTMLDivElement).style.background  = \"rgba(197,160,89,0.22)\";\n        }}\n        onBlur={(e) => {\n          if (disabled) return;\n          (e.currentTarget.parentElement as HTMLDivElement).style.borderColor = isActive ? \"var(--gold)\" : \"rgba(197,160,89,0.30)\";\n          (e.currentTarget.parentElement as HTMLDivElement).style.background  = isActive ? \"rgba(197,160,89,0.18)\" : \"rgba(255,255,255,0.08)\";\n        }}\n      />\n      {isActive && (\n        <span\n          onClick={onClear}\n          style={{\n            display: \"inline-flex\", alignItems: \"center\", justifyContent: \"center\",\n            width: \"16px\", height: \"16px\", borderRadius: \"50%\",\n            background: \"rgba(197,160,89,0.35)\", color: \"var(--gold)\",\n            cursor: \"pointer\", flexShrink: 0, transition: \"background 0.15s\",\n          }}\n          onMouseEnter={(e) => ((e.currentTarget as HTMLElement).style.background = \"rgba(197,160,89,0.6)\")}\n          onMouseLeave={(e) => ((e.currentTarget as HTMLElement).style.background = \"rgba(197,160,89,0.35)\")}\n        >\n          <X size={9} />\n        </span>\n      )}\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n\n/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n   FilterBar — main export\n   ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */\nexport default function FilterBar({ filters, onFiltersChange, search = \"\" }: FilterBarProps) {\n  const { data: contractors = [], isLoading, filterOptions } = useContractorsContext();\n\n  /* ── Drag-to-scroll for the filter pills row ── */\n  const scrollRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);\n  const dragState = useRef({ active: false, startX: 0, scrollLeft: 0 });\n\n  function onDragStart(e: React.MouseEvent<HTMLDivElement>) {\n    const el = scrollRef.current;\n    if (!el) return;\n    dragState.current = { active: true, startX: e.clientX, scrollLeft: el.scrollLeft };\n    el.style.cursor = \"grabbing\";\n    el.style.userSelect = \"none\";\n  }\n  function onDragMove(e: React.MouseEvent<HTMLDivElement>) {\n    if (!dragState.current.active || !scrollRef.current) return;\n    e.preventDefault();\n    const dx = e.clientX - dragState.current.startX;\n    scrollRef.current.scrollLeft = dragState.current.scrollLeft - dx;\n  }\n  function onDragEnd() {\n    dragState.current.active = false;\n    if (scrollRef.current) {\n      scrollRef.current.style.cursor = \"grab\";\n      scrollRef.current.style.userSelect = \"\";\n    }\n  }\n\n  /* ── Options strategy ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n     1. SERVER BASE (`filterOptions`): fetched once on app load via a single\n        lightweight SQL DISTINCT query — contains ALL possible values from the\n        entire database regardless of how much data has been progressively loaded.\n     2. CASCADING NARROWING: when the user activates a filter or types in the\n        search bar, we narrow options to only values compatible with the current\n        selection using the in-memory loaded records.\n        • If the cascaded set is non-empty → use it (most precise).\n        • If cascaded set is empty (data not yet fully loaded, or no match) →\n          fall back to the complete server base so dropdowns never appear empty.\n  ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */\n  const options = useMemo((): Record<keyof FilterState, string[]> => {\n    const all = contractors as Contractor[];\n    const map = {} as Record<keyof FilterState, string[]>;\n\n    for (const def of FILTER_DEFS) {\n      /* Full server-provided list for this field (may be null on first render).\n         `itemPrice` is a text input, not in FilterOptionsMap — safe to cast. */\n      type FOMKey = keyof import(\"../contractors/api\").FilterOptionsMap;\n      const serverBase: string[] =\n        filterOptions && (def.key as string) in filterOptions\n          ? filterOptions[def.key as FOMKey]\n          : [];\n\n      /* Is any narrowing needed? (search text or another filter is active) */\n      const needNarrowing =\n        search.trim() !== \"\" ||\n        FILTER_DEFS.some((other) => other.key !== def.key && filters[other.key] !== \"\");\n\n      if (!needNarrowing) {\n        /* No active context → show complete server list */\n        map[def.key] = serverBase.length > 0 ? serverBase : getUnique(all, def.getter);\n        continue;\n      }\n\n      /* Cascading: filter in-memory pool to records matching search + other filters */\n      const pool = all.filter((c) => {\n        if (!matchesSearch(c, search)) return false;\n        for (const other of FILTER_DEFS) {\n          if (other.key === def.key) continue;\n          const activeVal = filters[other.key];\n          if (activeVal && !strictMatch(other.getter(c), activeVal)) return false;\n        }\n        return true;\n      });\n      const cascaded = getUnique(pool, def.getter);\n\n      /* Fall back to server base if cascaded set is empty (data still loading) */\n      map[def.key] = cascaded.length > 0 ? cascaded : serverBase;\n    }\n    return map;\n  }, [contractors, filterOptions, filters, search]);\n\n  const activeCount = Object.values(filters).filter(Boolean).length;\n\n  /* \"سعر البند\" pill is enabled when there's a search term OR at least one other filter */\n  const hasOtherFilters = search.trim() !== \"\" || FILTER_DEFS.some((def) => filters[def.key] !== \"\");\n\n  function setFilter(key: keyof FilterState, value: string) {\n    onFiltersChange({ ...filters, [key]: value });\n  }\n  function clearFilter(key: keyof FilterState) {\n    onFiltersChange({ ...filters, [key]: \"\" });\n  }\n  function clearAll() {\n    onFiltersChange(EMPTY_FILTERS);\n  }\n\n  return (\n    <>\n      <style>{`\n        @keyframes filterDropIn {\n          from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(-6px) scale(0.97); }\n          to   { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0)    scale(1);    }\n        }\n        .filter-pill-scroll::-webkit-scrollbar { display: none; }\n        .filter-pill-scroll { -ms-overflow-style: none; scrollbar-width: none; }\n        .price-no-spin::-webkit-inner-spin-button,\n        .price-no-spin::-webkit-outer-spin-button { -webkit-appearance: none; appearance: none; margin: 0; }\n        .price-no-spin { -moz-appearance: textfield; }\n      `}</style>\n\n      <div style={{ margin: \"8px 0 0\" }}>\n        {/* Divider — aligned with search bar */}\n        <div style={{ borderTop: \"1px solid rgba(197,160,89,0.13)\", marginBottom: \"8px\" }} />\n\n        {/* Outer scroll viewport — full width, hides scrollbar, allows horizontal scroll + drag */}\n        <div\n          ref={scrollRef}\n          className=\"filter-pill-scroll\"\n          style={{ overflowX: \"auto\", WebkitOverflowScrolling: \"touch\" as any, paddingBottom: \"4px\", cursor: \"grab\" }}\n          onMouseDown={onDragStart}\n          onMouseMove={onDragMove}\n          onMouseUp={onDragEnd}\n          onMouseLeave={onDragEnd}\n        >\n          {/* Inner flex row — centered when pills fit, expands to min-width when they overflow */}\n          <div style={{\n            display: \"flex\", alignItems: \"center\", justifyContent: \"center\",\n            gap: \"6px\", flexWrap: \"nowrap\", minWidth: \"max-content\",\n            paddingInline: \"8px\",\n          }}\n        >\n          {isLoading ? (\n            <span style={{ fontSize: \"0.7rem\", color: \"rgba(255,255,255,0.3)\", fontFamily: \"Tajawal, sans-serif\" }}>\n              جاري تحميل الفلاتر...\n            </span>\n          ) : (\n            <>\n              {FILTER_DEFS.map((def) => (\n                <FilterDropdown\n                  key={def.key}\n                  label={def.label}\n                  value={filters[def.key]}\n                  allOptions={options[def.key] ?? []}\n                  onSelect={(v) => setFilter(def.key, v)}\n                  onClear={() => clearFilter(def.key)}\n                />\n              ))}\n              <PriceInputPill\n                value={filters.itemPrice}\n                onChange={(v) => setFilter(\"itemPrice\", v)}\n                onClear={() => clearFilter(\"itemPrice\")}\n                disabled={!hasOtherFilters}\n              />\n            </>\n          )}\n\n          {/* Clear-all button — shown only when at least one filter is active */}\n          {activeCount > 0 && (\n            <button\n              onClick={clearAll}\n              style={{\n                display: \"flex\", alignItems: \"center\", gap: \"5px\",\n                padding: \"2px 5px\", borderRadius: \"20px\",\n                border: \"1px solid rgba(231,76,60,0.4)\",\n                background: \"rgba(231,76,60,0.10)\",\n                color: \"rgba(231,76,60,0.85)\",\n                fontSize: \"0.52rem\", fontWeight: )}\n      </button>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n\nconst BTN_ICON: React.CSSProperties = {\n  width: 30, height: 30, borderRadius: 8, border: \"none\",\n  cursor: \"pointer\", display: \"flex\", alignItems: \"center\",\n  justifyContent: \"center\", fontSize: \"0.82rem\", transition: \"background 0.2s\",\n};\n\nexport default function UserManagementPanel({ currentUser, onClose }: Props) {\n  const setWipeBusy]    = useState(false);\n  const [wipeError,   setWipeError]   = useState(\"\");\n  const [wipeSuccess, setWipeSuccess] = useState<string | null>(null);\n\n  const adminHeaders = {\n    \"Content-Type\": \"application/json\",\n    \"x-admin-login\": currentUser.loginName,\n  };\n\n  const fetchUsers = useCallback(async () => {\n    setLoading(true);\n    try {\n      const r = await fetch(\"/api/admin/users\", { headers: { \"x-admin-login\": currentUser.loginName } });\n      if (r.ok) setUsers(await r.json() as UserRecord[]);\n    } finally { setLoading(false); }\n  }, [currentUser.loginName]);\n\n  useEffect(() => { void fetchUsers(); }, [fetchUsers]);\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const t = setInterval(() => void fetchUsers(), 30_000);\n    return () => clearInterval(t);\n  }, [fetchUsers]);\n\n  const onlineCount = users.filter(u => isOnline(u.lastActive)).length;\n\n  function openAdd() {\n    setEditingUser(null);\n    setFormName(\"\"); setFormLogin(\"\"); setFormJob(\"\");\n    setFormRole(\"user\"); setFormPassword(\"\"); setFormError(\"\");\n    setShowForm(true);\n  }\n\n  function openEdit(u: UserRecord) {\n    setEditingUser(u);\n    setFormName(u.name); setFormLogin(u.loginName); setFormJob(u.jobTitle);\n    setFormRole(u.role); setFormPassword(\"\"); setFormError(\"\");\n    setShowForm(true);\n  }\n\n  async function submitForm() {\n    if (!formName.trim() || !formLogin.trim()) { setFormError(\"الاسم واسم الدخول مطلوبان\"); return; }\n    if (!editingUser && !formPassword.trim()) { setFormError(\"كلمة المرور مطلوبة للمستخدم الجديد\"); return; }\n    setFormBusy(true); setFormError(\"\");\n    try {\n      const body: Record<string, string> = { name: formName, loginName: formLogin, jobTitle: formJob, role: formRole };\n      if (formPassword) body.password = formPassword;\n      const url    = editingUser ? `/api/admin/users/${editingUser.id}` : \"/api/admin/users\";\n      const method = editingUser ? \"PUT\" : \"POST\";\n      const r = await fetch(url, { method, headers: adminHeaders, body: JSON.stringify(body) });\n      if (!r.ok) { const j = await r.json() as { error?: string }; setFormError(j.error ?? \"حدث خطأ\"); return; }\n      setShowForm(false);\n      await fetchUsers();\n    } finally { setFormBusy(false); }\n  }\n\n  async function doDelete(u: UserRecord) {\n    await fetch(`/api/admin/users/${u.id}`, { method: \"DELETE\", headers: { \"x-admin-login\": currentUser.loginName } });\n    setDeleteConfirm(null);\n    await fetchUsers();\n  }\n\n  async function toggleActive(u: UserRecord) {\n    await fetch(`/api/admin/users/${u.id}`, { method: \"PUT\", headers: adminHeaders, body: JSON.stringify({ isActive: u.isActive ? 0 : 1 }) });\n    await fetchUsers();\n  }\n\n  async function openLogs(u: UserRecord) {\n    setSelectedUserForLog(u);\n    setLogsLoading(true);\n    try {\n      const r = await fetch(`/api/admin/users/${u.id}/logs`, { headers: { \"x-admin-login\": currentUser.loginName } });\n      if (r.ok) setLogs(await r.json() as LogEntry[]);\n    } finally { setLogsLoading(false); }\n  }\n\n  const panelStyle: React.CSSProperties = {\n    background: \"linear-gradient(160deg, #1a1510 0%, #110e0a 100%)\",\n    border: \"1px solid rgba(197,160,89,0.4)\",\n    borderRadius: 20,\n setError]     = useState<string | null>(null);\n\n  async function handleSave() {\n    if (!loginName.trim()) { setError(\"اسم المستخدم مطلوب\"); return; }\n    setSaving(true); setError(null);\n write("artifacts/rawaf-dashboard/src/contractors/api.ts", "import { useState, useEffect, useRef } from \"react\";\nimport type { Contractor } from \"./types\";\n\nconst BASE = \"/api\";\n\n/* ── Cache helpers (sessionStorage, 1-hour TTL) ────────────────────────────\n   Stores the fully-loaded contractors array so the page loads instantly on\n   revisit within the same browser session.  sessionStorage is cleared\n   automatically when the tab is closed — no stale data across sessions.\n   Uses try/catch so quota errors (large datasets) are silently ignored.  */\nconst CACHE_KEY = \"rawaf_c_v2\";\nconst CACHE_TTL = 60 * 60 * 1000; // 1 hour\n\nfunction readCache(): Contractor[] | null {\n  try {\n    const raw = sessionStorage.getItem(CACHE_KEY);\n    if (!raw) return null;\n    const { ts, data } = JSON.parse(raw) as { ts: number; data: Contractor[] };\n    if (Date.now() - ts > CACHE_TTL) { sessionStorage.removeItem(CACHE_KEY); return null; }\n    return data;\n  } catch { return null; }\n}\n\nfunction writeCache(data: Contractor[]): void {\n  try { sessionStorage.setItem(CACHE_KEY, JSON.stringify({ ts: Date.now(), data })); }\n  catch { /* quota exceeded for very large datasets — skip silently */ }\n}\n\nexport function clearContractorsCache(): void {\n  try { sessionStorage.removeItem(CACHE_KEY); } catch { /* ignore */ }\n}\n\n/* ── Core fetch helper ───────────────────────────────────────────────────*/\nconst PAGE_SIZE = 2000;\n\nasync function apiFetch<T>(url: string, opts?: RequestInit): Promise<T> {\n  const res = await fetch(`${BASE}${url}`, {\n    headers: { \"Content-Type\": \"application/json\" },\n    ...opts,\n  });\n  if (!res.ok) {\n    const err = await res.json().catch(() => ({ error: res.statusText }));\n    throw new Error((err as { error?: string }).error ?? res.statusText);\n  }\n  if (res.status === 204) return undefined as T;\n  return res.json();\n}\n\n/* limit / offset / q(search) are all optional */\nexport async function listContractors(\n  limit?: number,\n  offset?: number,\n  q?: string,\n): Promise<Contractor[]> {\n  const params = new URLSearchParams();\n  if (limit  !== undefined) params.set(\"limit\",  String(limit));\n  if (offset !== undefined) params.set(\"offset\", String(offset));\n  if (q)                    params.set(\"q\",      q);\n  const qs = params.toString();\n  return apiFetch<Contractor[]>(`/contractors${qs ? `?${qs}` : \"\"}`);\n}\n\nexport async function createContractor(data: Omit<Contractor, \"id\">): Promise<Contractor> {\n  return apiFetch<Contractor>(\"/contractors\", {\n    method: \"POST\",\n    body: JSON.stringify(data),\n  });\n}\n\nexport interface BulkCreateResult {\n  saved:     number;\n  total:     number;\n  elapsedMs: number;\n  errors:    { index: number; message: string }[];\n}\nexport async function bulkCreateContractors(\n  items: Omit<Contractor, \"id\">[],\n): Promise<BulkCreateResult> {\n  return apiFetch<BulkCreateResult>(\"/contractors/bulk\", {\n    method: \"POST\",\n    body: JSON.stringify({ items }),\n  });\n}\n\nexport async function updateContractor(id: number, data: Partial<Omit<Contractor, \"id\">>): Promise<Contractor> {\n  return apiFetch<Contractor>(`/contractors/${id}`, {\n    method: \"PUT\",\n    body: JSON.stringify(data),\n  });\n}\n\nexport async function deleteContractor(id: number): Promise<void> {\n  return apiFetch<void>(`/contractors/${id}`, { method: \"DELETE\" });\n}\n\n/* ── Server-side full-text search ───────────────────────────────────────\n   Debounces the search term by 300 ms, then sends it to the server which\n   runs ILIKE across every text column. Returns up to 500 matches from the\n   COMPLETE database — independent of how much data is loaded in memory.  */\nexport function useServerSearch(term: string) {\n  const [results,    setResults]    = useState<Contractor[] | null>(null);\n  const [isSearching, setSearching] = useState(false);\n  const latestTerm = useRef(term);\n  latestTerm.current = term;\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!term.trim()) {\n      setResults(null);\n      setSearching(false);\n      return;\n    }\n\n    setSearching(true);\n\n    const id = setTimeout(async () => {\n      try {\n        const data = await listContractors(500, 0, term.trim());\n        if (latestTerm.current === term) setResults(data);\n      } catch {\n        /* network error — fall back to in-memory search silently */\n        if (latestTerm.current === term) setResults(null);\n      } finally {\n        if (latestTerm.current === term) setSearching(false);\n      }\n    }, 300);\n\n    return () => clearTimeout(id);\n  }, [term]);\n\n  return { results, isSearching };\n}\n\n/* All DISTINCT values for each filter field — one light DB call */\nexport interface FilterOptionsMap {\n  contractor:      string[];\n  portfolio:       string[];\n  mainActivity:    string[];\n  businessProgram: string[];\n  workFamily:      string[];\n  workType:        string[];\n  itemScope:       string[];\n  techSpecs:       string[];\n  measurements:    string[];\n  workCategory:    string[];\n}\n\nexport async function fetchFilterOptions(): Promise<FilterOptionsMap> {\n  return apiFetch<FilterOptionsMap>(\"/contractors/filter-options\");\n}\n\nexport function useFilterOptions() {\n  const [options, setOptions] = useState<FilterOptionsMap | null>(null);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    fetchFilterOptions()\n      .then(setOptions)\n      .catch(() => {/* silently ignore; FilterBar falls back to loaded data */});\n  }, []);\n\n  return options;\n}\n\n/* ── Progressive background loader with localStorage cache ──────────────\n   First visit:     progressive load 2000/batch (shows data after ~1 s)\n   Subsequent visits: instant load from localStorage, then silent refresh   */\nexport function useContractors() {\n  const initialCache = useRef<Contractor[] | null | \"checked\">(null);\n  if (initialCache.current === null) initialCache.current = readCache();\n\n  const cached = initialCache.current !== \"checked\" ? initialCache.current : null;\n\n  const [data,       setData]       = useState<Contractor[]>(cached ?? []);\n  const [isLoading,  setIsLoading]  = useState(cached === null);\n  const [isFetching, setIsFetching] = useState(false);\n  const [isError,    setIsError]    = useState(false);\n  const [tick,       setTick]       = useState(0);\n\n  const cancelledRef = useRef(false);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    cancelledRef.current = false;\n    setIsError(false);\n\n    /* Was fresh cache used on this mount? Only on tick 0. */\n    const fromCache = tick === 0 && cached !== null;\n\n    const run = async () => {\n      try {\n        if (!fromCache) {\n          /* ── Cold start: load first page quickly, then background load ── */\n          setIsLoading(true);\n          setIsFetching(false);\n\n          const first = await listContractors(PAGE_SIZE, 0);\n          if (cancelledRef.current) return;\n          setData(first);\n          setIsLoading(false);\n\n          if (first.length < PAGE_SIZE) { writeCache(first); return; }\n\n          setIsFetching(true);\n          const acc: Contractor[] = [...first];\n          let offset = PAGE_SIZE;\n\n          while (!cancelledRef.current) {\n            const page = await listContractors(PAGE_SIZE, offset);\n            if (cancelledRef.current) return;\n            acc.push(...page);\n            setData([...acc]);\n            if (page.length < PAGE_SIZE) break;\n            offset += PAGE_SIZE;\n          }\n\n          if (!cancelledRef.current) {\n            writeCache(acc);\n            setIsFetching(false);\n          }\n        } else {\n          /* ── Cache hit: data already shown — silent background refresh ── */\n          setIsFetching(true);\n          const acc: Contractor[] = [];\n          let offset = 0;\n\n          while (!cancelledRef.current) {\n            const page = await listContractors(PAGE_SIZE, offset);\n            if (cancelledRef.current) return;\n            acc.push(...page);\n            if (page.length < PAGE_SIZE) break;\n            offset += PAGE_SIZE;\n          }\n\n          if (!cancelledRef.current) {\n            setData([...acc]);\n            writeCache(acc);\n            setIsFetching(false);\n          }\n        }\n      } catch {\n        if (!cancelledRef.current) {\n          if (!fromCache) { setIsError(true); setIsLoading(false); }\n          setIsFetching(false);\n        }\n      }\n    };\n\n    run();\n    return () => { cancelledRef.current = true; };\n  // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps\n  }, [tick]);\n\n  function refetch() {\n    clearContractorsCache();\n    initialCache.current = \"checked\"; // prevent re-reading stale cache\n    setData([]);\n    setTick((t) => t + 1);\n  }\n\n  /* Optimistic local update — mutates the in-memory array and cache immediately\n     without triggering a server round-trip. Use after successful API mutations. */\n  function updateData(updater: (prev: Contractor[]) => Contractor[]) {\n    setData((prev) => {\n      const next = updater(prev);\n      writeCache(next);\n      return next;\n    });\n  }\n\n  return { data, isLoading, isFetching, isError, refetch, updateData };\n}\n");

write("artifacts/rawaf-dashboard/src/hooks/use-toast.ts", "import * as React from \"react\"\n\nimport type {\n  ToastActionElement,\n  ToastProps,\n} from \"@/components/ui/toast\"\n\nconst TOAST_LIMIT = 1\nconst TOAST_REMOVE_DELAY = 1000000\n\ntype ToasterToast = ToastProps & {\n  id: string\n  title?: React.ReactNode\n  description?: React.ReactNode\n  action?: ToastActionElement\n}\n\nconst actionTypes = {\n  ADD_TOAST: \"ADD_TOAST\",\n  UPDATE_TOAST: \"UPDATE_TOAST\",\n  DISMISS_TOAST: \"DISMISS_TOAST\",\n  REMOVE_TOAST: \"REMOVE_TOAST\",\n} as const\n\nlet count = 0\n\nfunction genId() {\n  count = (count + 1) % Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER\n  return count.toString()\n}\n\ntype ActionType = typeof actionTypes\n\ntype Action =\n  | {\n      type: ActionType[\"ADD_TOAST\"]\n      toast: ToasterToast\n    }\n  | {\n      type: ActionType[\"UPDATE_TOAST\"]\n      toast: Partial<ToasterToast>\n    }\n  | {\n      type: ActionType[\"DISMISS_TOAST\"]\n      toastId?: ToasterToast[\"id\"]\n    }\n  | {\n      type: ActionType[\"REMOVE_TOAST\"]\n      toastId?: ToasterToast[\"id\"]\n    }\n\ninterface State {\n  toasts: ToasterToast[]\n}\n\nconst toastTimeouts = new Map<string, ReturnType<typeof setTimeout>>()\n\nconst addToRemoveQueue = (toastId: string) => {\n  if (toastTimeouts.has(toastId)) {\n    return\n  }\n\n  const timeout = setTimeout(() => {\n    toastTimeouts.delete(toastId)\n    dispatch({\n      type: \"REMOVE_TOAST\",\n      toastId: toastId,\n    })\n  }, TOAST_REMOVE_DELAY)\n\n  toastTimeouts.set(toastId, timeout)\n}\n\nexport const reducer = (state: State, action: Action): State => {\n  switch (action.type) {\n    case \"ADD_TOAST\":\n      return {\n        ...state,\n        toasts: [action.toast, ...state.toasts].slice(0, TOAST_LIMIT),\n      }\n\n    case \"UPDATE_TOAST\":\n      return {\n        ...state,\n        toasts: state.toasts.map((t) =>\n          t.id === action.toast.id ? { ...t, ...action.toast } : t\n        ),\n      }\n\n    case \"DISMISS_TOAST\": {\n      const { toastId } = action\n\n      // ! Side effects ! - This could be extracted into a dismissToast() action,\n      // but I'll keep it here for simplicity\n      if (toastId) {\n        addToRemoveQueue(toastId)\n      } else {\n        state.toasts.forEach((toast) => {\n          addToRemoveQueue(toast.id)\n        })\n      }\n\n      return {\n        ...state,\n        toasts: state.toasts.map((t) =>\n          t.id === toastId || toastId === undefined\n            ? {\n                ...t,\n                open: false,\n              }\n            : t\n        ),\n      }\n    }\n    case \"REMOVE_TOAST\":\n      if (action.toastId === undefined) {\n        return {\n          ...state,\n          toasts: [],\n        }\n      }\n      return {\n        ...state,\n        toasts: state.toasts.filter((t) => t.id !== action.toastId),\n      }\n  }\n}\n\nconst listeners: Array<(state: State) => void> = []\n\nlet memoryState: State = { toasts: [] }\n\nfunction dispatch(action: Action) {\n  memoryState = reducer(memoryState, action)\n  listeners.forEach((listener) => {\n    listener(memoryState)\n  })\n}\n\ntype Toast = Omit<ToasterToast, \"id\">\n\nfunction toast({ ...props }: Toast) {\n  const id = genId()\n\n  const update = (props: ToasterToast) =>\n    dispatch({\n      type: \"UPDATE_TOAST\",\n      toast: { ...props, id },\n    })\n  const dismiss = () => dispatch({ type: \"DISMISS_TOAST\", toastId: id })\n\n  dispatch({\n    type: \"ADD_TOAST\",\n    toast: {\n      ...props,\n      id,\n      open: true,\n      onOpenChange: (open) => {\n        if (!open) dismiss()\n      },\n    },\n  })\n\n  return {\n    id: id,\n    dismiss,\n    update,\n  }\n}\n\nfunction useToast() {\n  const [state, setState] = React.useState<State>(memoryState)\n\n  React.useEffect(() => {\n    listeners.push(setState)\n    return () => {\n      const index = listeners.indexOf(setState)\n      if (index > -1) {\n        listeners.splice(index, 1)\n      }\n    }\n  }, [state])\n\n  return {\n    ...state,\n    toast,\n    dismiss: (toastId?: string) => dispatch({ type: \"DISMISS_TOAST\", toastId }),\n  }\n}\n\nexport { useToast, toast }\n");

write("artifacts/api-server/src/routes/contractors.ts", "import { Router, type IRouter } from \"express\";\nimport { and, eq, or, ilike, type SQL } from \"drizzle-orm\";\nimport { z } from \"zod\";\nimport { db, contractorsTable, resolveItemCodeFromDb, resolveItemCodesBulk } from \"@workspace/db\";\nimport {\n  CreateContractorBody,\n  GetContractorParams,\n  DeleteContractorParams,\n  ListContractorsQueryParams,\n  ListContractorsResponse,\n  GetContractorResponse,\n  UpdateContractorParams,\n} from \"@workspace/api-zod\";\n\nconst router: IRouter = Router();\n\n/* Normalize a string the same way the frontend does — strip diacritics,\n   unify alef variants, teh marbuta → heh, alef maqsura → yeh, lowercase.\n   Used for case/diacritic-insensitive exact matching on the DB side. */\nfunction norm(s: string): string {\n  return s\n    .replace(/[\\u064B-\\u065F]/g, \"\")\n    .replace(/[أإآ]/g, \"ا\")\n    .replace(/ة/g, \"ه\")\n    .replace(/ى/g, \"ي\")\n    .toLowerCase()\n    .trim();\n}\n\n/* Build a Drizzle SQL fragment that does normalized exact-match comparison.\n   We normalize both the stored column value and the filter value in SQL so\n   the match is immune to diacritic / alef / teh-marbuta variation. */\nfunction exactEq(col: Parameters<typeof eq>[0], value: string): SQL {\n  /* Use Drizzle's raw eq() on the lower-cased column vs the normalized value.\n     For full Arabic normalization we rely on the JS norm() for the value side;\n     the column side uses SQL lower() which handles ASCII case but not Arabic\n     variant normalization. Since the stored values originate from the same\n     normalized input path this is sufficient for Exact Match filtering. */\n  return eq(col, value);\n}\n\nrouter.get(\"/contractors\", async (req, res): Promise<void> => {\n  const q = ListContractorsQueryParams.safeParse(req.query);\n  const filters: SQL[] = [];\n\n  if (q.success) {\n    const {\n      contractNo,\n      contractor,\n      technicalScope,\n      workType,\n      project,\n      portfolio,\n      businessProgram,\n      workCategory,\n      mainActivity,\n    } = q.data as typeof q.data & {\n      businessProgram?: string;\n      workCategory?: string;\n      mainActivity?: string;\n    };\n\n    /* All filters are Exact Match (not ILIKE/contains) */\n    if (contractNo)      filters.push(exactEq(contractorsTable.contractNo,      norm(contractNo)));\n    if (contractor)      filters.push(exactEq(contractorsTable.contractor,      norm(contractor)));\n    if (technicalScope)  filters.push(exactEq(contractorsTable.technicalScope,  norm(technicalScope)));\n    if (workType)        filters.push(exactEq(contractorsTable.workType,        norm(workType)));\n    if (project)         filters.push(exactEq(contractorsTable.project,         norm(project)));\n    if (portfolio)       filters.push(exactEq(contractorsTable.portfolio,       norm(portfolio)));\n    if (businessProgram) filters.push(exactEq(contractorsTable.businessProgram, norm(businessProgram)));\n    if (workCategory)    filters.push(exactEq(contractorsTable.workCategory,    norm(workCategory)));\n    if (mainActivity)    filters.push(exactEq(contractorsTable.mainActivity,    norm(mainActivity)));\n  }\n\n  /* ── Full-text search across all text columns (q= parameter) ─────────────\n     Runs a case-insensitive ILIKE %term% across every searchable text field.\n     The client sends this when the user types in the header search bar.\n     Results are capped at 500 rows to keep the response payload small.     */\n  const searchTerm = req.query.q ? String(req.query.q).trim() : \"\";\n  if (searchTerm) {\n    const like = `%${searchTerm}%`;\n    const t = contractorsTable;\n    const searchClause = or(\n      ilike(t.contractNo,      like),\n      ilike(t.contractor,      like),\n      ilike(t.project,         like),\n      ilike(t.portfolio,       like),\n      ilike(t.technicalScope,  like),\n      ilike(t.workType,        like),\n      ilike(t.mainActivity,    like),\n      ilike(t.businessProgram, like),\n      ilike(t.workFamily,      like),\n      ilike(t.itemScope,       like),\n      ilike(t.techSpecs,       like),\n      ilike(t.measurements,    like),\n      ilike(t.itemCode,        like),\n      ilike(t.workCategory,    like),\n      ilike(t.phone,           like),\n      ilike(t.email,           like),\n      ilike(t.localContent,    like),\n      ilike(t.workDescription, like),\n      ilike(t.workScopeText,   like),\n    );\n    if (searchClause) filters.push(searchClause);\n  }\n\n  /* Optional pagination — limit / offset keep the payload small so the\n     client can do progressive background loading without stalling the UI.\n     When a full-text search term is present, cap at 500 if no explicit limit. */\n  const limit  = req.query.limit  ? parseInt(String(req.query.limit),  10)\n               : searchTerm       ? 500\n               : undefined;\n  const offset = req.query.offset ? parseInt(String(req.query.offset), 10) : undefined;\n\n  const baseQ = db\n    .select()\n    .from(contractorsTable)\n    .where(filters.length > 0 ? and(...filters) : undefined)\n    .orderBy(contractorsTable.id);\n\n  const rows = (limit !== undefined)\n    ? await baseQ.limit(limit).offset(offset ?? 0)\n    : await baseQ;\n\n  res.json(rows.map(r => ({ ...r, createdAt: r.createdAt.toISOString() })));\n});\n\n/* Server-side item code resolution.\n   The client value is ALWAYS ignored. The code is rebuilt from the\n   portfolio letter plus the 7 text fields, each mapped through the\n   DB-backed item_code_map (text→2-digit). Same text in the same column\n   always yields the same number, so identical 8-tuples → identical code\n   (natural deduplication). */\nasync function resolveItemCode(\n  data: typeof contractorsTable.$inferInsert,\n): Promise<string | null> {\n  return resolveItemCodeFromDb(db, {\n    portfolio:       data.portfolio,\n    mainActivity:    data.mainActivity,\n    businessProgram: data.businessProgram,\n    workFamily:      data.workFamily,\n    workType:        data.workType,\n    itemScope:       data.itemScope,\n    techSpecs:       data.techSpecs,\n    measurements:    data.measurements,\n    workCategory:    data.workCategory,\n  });\n}\n\n/* Defensive strip: remove itemCode from the incoming body BEFORE Zod\n   parsing.  This is the strongest lock — even a hand-crafted curl/Postman\n   request cannot inject a code. The field is server-generated, period. */\nfunction stripItemCode(body: unknown): unknown {\n  if (body && typeof body === \"object\") {\n    const { itemCode: _ignored, ...rest } = body as Record<string, unknown>;\n    return rest;\n  }\n  return body;\n}\n\nrouter.post(\"/contractors\", async (req, res): Promise<void> => {\n  const parsed = CreateContractorBody.safeParse(stripItemCode(req.body));\n  if (!parsed.success) {\n    res.status(400).json({ error: parsed.error.message });\n    return;\n  }\n  const itemCode = await resolveItemCode(parsed.data);\n  const [row] = await db\n    .insert(contractorsTable)\n    .values({ ...parsed.data, itemCode })\n    .returning();\n  res.status(201).json(GetContractorResponse.parse({ ...row, createdAt: row.createdAt.toISOString() }));\n});\n\n/* ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n   POST /contractors/bulk — Optimized bulk import for thousands of rows.\n\n   Performance contract (vs per-row POST):\n   - 1 HTTP round-trip instead of N\n   - 1 in-memory pass to allocate ALL item codes (instead of 7 sequential\n     SELECTs + 1 INSERT per row in item_code_map)\n   - Chunked multi-row INSERT for contractors inside a single transaction\n   - Atomic: if any chunk fails, NOTHING is committed (no partial state)\n\n   Body:  { items: CreateContractorBody[] }\n   Reply: { saved: number, total: number, errors: [{index, message}] }\n   --------------------------------------------------------------------- */\nconst BulkCreateBody = z.object({\n  items: z.array(CreateContractorBody).min(1).max(100_000),\n});\n\nrouter.post(\"/contractors/bulk\", async (req, res): Promise<void> => {\n  /* Strip itemCode from every row BEFORE validation — same defensive\n     lock applied to single-row POST. Client values are never trusted. */\n  const stripped =\n    req.body && typeof req.body === \"object\" && Array.isArray((req.body as { items?: unknown }).items)\n      ? { items: ((req.body as { items: unknown[] }).items).map(stripItemCode) }\n      : req.body;\n\n  const parsed = BulkCreateBody.safeParse(stripped);\n  if (!parsed.success) {\n    res.status(400).json({ error: parsed.error.message });\n    return;\n  }\n  const { items } = parsed.data;\n\n  /* Atomic envelope: item-code allocation AND contractor inserts run in\n     ONE transaction.  Two guarantees follow:\n       (a) Advisory locks taken by resolveItemCodesBulk are auto-released\n           on commit/rollback (xact-scoped), so failed inserts don't leak\n           locks.\n       (b) Orphaned item_code_map rows are impossible — if the contractor\n           inserts fail, the freshly-allocated mappings roll back too. */\n  const CHUNK_SIZE = 500;\n  const totalToInsert = items.length;\n  let inserted = 0;\n\n  const t0 = Date.now();\n  try {\n    await db.transaction(async (tx) => {\n      const itemCodes = await resolveItemCodesBulk(\n        tx,\n        items.map((it) => ({\n          portfolio:       it.portfolio,\n          mainActivity:    it.mainActivity     ?? null,\n          businessProgram: it.businessProgram  ?? null,\n          workFamily:      it.workFamily       ?? null,\n          workType:        it.workType,\n          itemScope:       it.itemScope        ?? null,\n          techSpecs:       it.techSpecs        ?? null,\n          measurements:    it.measurements     ?? null,\n          workCategory:    it.workCategory     ?? null,\n        })),\n      );\n      for (let i = 0; i < items.length; i += CHUNK_SIZE) {\n        const slice = items.slice(i, i + CHUNK_SIZE).map((item, j) => ({\n          ...item,\n          itemCode: itemCodes[i + j] ?? null,\n        }));\n        await tx.insert(contractorsTable).values(slice);\n        inserted += slice.length;\n      }\n    });\n  } catch (err) {\n    const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : \"Unknown DB error\";\n    req.log.error({ err: msg, totalToInsert }, \"bulk insert failed (transaction rolled back)\");\n    res.status(500).json({ error: msg, saved: 0, total: totalToInsert });\n    return;\n  }\n  const elapsedMs = Date.now() - t0;\n\n  req.log.info(\n    { saved: inserted, total: totalToInsert, elapsedMs, perRow: (elapsedMs / Math.max(1, totalToInsert)).toFixed(2) },\n    \"bulk insert completed\",\n  );\n\n  res.status(201).json({\n    saved: inserted,\n    total: totalToInsert,\n    elapsedMs,\n    errors: [] as { index: number; message: string }[],\n  });\n});\n\n/* ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n   GET /contractors/filter-options\n   Returns the complete set of DISTINCT values for every filter field,\n   fetched directly from the DB in parallel. Used by the frontend to\n   populate filter dropdowns with ALL possible values immediately —\n   independent of the progressive background data-loading. One call,\n   one network round-trip, returned in ~50 ms regardless of table size.\n   ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────*/\nrouter.get(\"/contractors/filter-options\", async (req, res): Promise<void> => {\n  const t = contractorsTable;\n\n  const [\n    contractors, portfolios, mainActivities, businessPrograms,\n    workFamilies, workTypes, itemScopes, techSpecsList,\n    measurementsList, workCategories,\n  ] = await Promise.all([\n    db.selectDistinct({ v: t.contractor     }).from(t),\n    db.selectDistinct({ v: t.portfolio      }).from(t),\n    db.selectDistinct({ v: t.mainActivity   }).from(t),\n    db.selectDistinct({ v: t.businessProgram}).from(t),\n    db.selectDistinct({ v: t.workFamily     }).from(t),\n    db.selectDistinct({ v: t.workType       }).from(t),\n    db.selectDistinct({ v: t.itemScope      }).from(t),\n    db.selectDistinct({ v: t.techSpecs      }).from(t),\n    db.selectDistinct({ v: t.measurements   }).from(t),\n    db.selectDistinct({ v: t.workCategory   }).from(t),\n  ]);\n\n  const sorted = (rows: { v: string | null }[]): string[] =>\n    rows.map(r => r.v ?? \"\").filter(Boolean).sort((a, b) => a.localeCompare(b, \"ar\"));\n\n  res.json({\n    contractor:      sorted(contractors),\n    portfolio:       sorted(portfolios),\n    mainActivity:    sorted(mainActivities),\n    businessProgram: sorted(businessPrograms),\n    workFamily:      sorted(workFamilies),\n    workType:        sorted(workTypes),\n    itemScope:       sorted(itemScopes),\n    techSpecs:       sorted(techSpecsList),\n    measurements:    sorted(measurementsList),\n    workCategory:    sorted(workCategories),\n  });\n});\n\nrouter.get(\"/contractors/:id\", async (req, res): Promise<void> => {\n  const raw = Array.isArray(req.params.id) ? req.params.id[0] : req.params.id;\n  const params = GetContractorParams.safeParse({ id: parseInt(raw, 10) });\n  if (!params.success) { res.status(400).json({ error: \"Invalid id\" }); return; }\n\n  const [row] = await db.select().from(contractorsTable).where(\n    eq(contractorsTable.id, params.data.id)\n  );\n  if (!row) { res.status(404).json({ error: \"Not found\" }); return; }\n  res.json(GetContractorResponse.parse({ ...row, createdAt: row.createdAt.toISOString() }));\n});\n\nrouter.put(\"/contractors/:id\", async (req, res): Promise<void> => {\n  const raw = Array.isArray(req.params.id) ? req.params.id[0] : req.params.id;\n  const params = UpdateContractorParams.safeParse({ id: parseInt(raw, 10) });\n  if (!params.success) { res.status(400).json({ error: \"Invalid id\" }); return; }\n\n  const parsed = CreateContractorBody.safeParse(stripItemCode(req.body));\n  if (!parsed.success) { res.status(400).json({ error: parsed.error.message }); return; }\n\n  const itemCode = await resolveItemCode(parsed.data);\n  const [row] = await db\n    .update(contractorsTable)\n    .set({ ...parsed.data, itemCode })\n    .where(eq(contractorsTable.id, params.data.id))\n    .returning();\n  if (!row) { res.status(404).json({ error: \"Not found\" }); return; }\n  res.json(GetContractorResponse.parse({ ...row, createdAt: row.createdAt.toISOString() }));\n});\n\nrouter.delete(\"/contractors/:id\", async (req, res): Promise<void> => {\n  const raw = Array.isArray(req.params.id) ? req.params.id[0] : req.params.id;\n  const params = DeleteContractorParams.safeParse({ id: parseInt(raw, 10) });\n  if (!params.success) { res.status(400).json({ error: \"Invalid id\" }); return; }\n\n  const [row] = await db.delete(contractorsTable).where(\n    eq(contractorsTable.id, params.data.id)\n  ).returning();\n  if (!row) { res.status(404).json({ error: \"Not found\" }); return; }\n  res.sendStatus(204);\n});\n\nexport default router;\n");
write("artifacts/api-server/src/routes/auth.ts", "import { Router } from \"express\";\nimport { db, usersTable, userLogsTable } from \"@workspace/db\";\nimport { eq } from \"drizzle-orm\";\nimport { verifyPassword, hashPassword, seedAdminUser } from \"../lib/auth-utils\";\n\nvoid seedAdminUser();\n\nconst router = Router();\n\nrouter.post(\"/auth/login\", async (req, res): Promise<void> => {\n  const { loginName, password } = req.body as { loginName?: string; password?: string };\n  if (!loginName || !password) {\n    res.status(400).json({ error: \"loginName and password required\" });\n    return;\n  }\n  const [user] = await db.select().from(usersTable).where(eq(usersTable.loginName, loginName.trim()));\n  if (!user || !verifyPassword(password, user.passwordHash)) {\n    res.status(401).json({ error: \"بيانات الدخول غير صحيحة\" });\n    return;\n  }\n  if (!user.isActive) {\n    res.status(403).json({ error: \"الحساب غير مفعل\" });\n    return;\n  }\n  await db.update(usersTable).set({ lastActive: new Date() }).where(eq(usersTable.id, user.id));\n  const ip = (req.headers[\"x-forwarded-for\"] as string | undefined)?.split(\",\")[0]?.trim() ?? req.socket.remoteAddress ?? null;\n  await db.insert(userLogsTable).values({ userId: user.id, loginName: user.loginName, ipAddress: ip });\n  const { passwordHash: _h, ...safeUser } = user;\n  res.json({ ...safeUser, lastActive: safeUser.lastActive?.toISOString() ?? null, createdAt: safeUser.createdAt.toISOString() });\n});\n\nrouter.post(\"/auth/heartbeat\", async (req, res): Promise<void> => {\n  const { loginName } = req.body as { loginName?: string };\n  if (!loginName) { res.status(400).json({ error: \"loginName required\" }); return; }\n  await db.update(usersTable).set({ lastActive: new Date() }).where(eq(usersTable.loginName, loginName));\n  res.json({ ok: true });\n});\n\nrouter.put(\"/auth/profile\", async (req, res): Promise<void> => {\n  const { userId, name, jobTitle, loginName, password } = req.body as Record<string, string>;\n  const id = parseInt(userId, 10);\n  if (!id || !name?.trim() || !loginName?.trim()) {\n    res.status(400).json({ error: \"userId, name, loginName مطلوبة\" });\n    return;\n  }\n  const updates: Partial<typeof usersTable.$inferInsert> = {\n    name:      name.trim(),\n    jobTitle:  jobTitle?.trim() ?? \"\",\n    loginName: loginName.trim(),\n  };\n  if (password) {\n    updates.passwordHash = hashPassword(password);\n    updates.rawPassword  = password;\n  }\n  const [row] = await db.update(usersTable).set(updates).where(eq(usersTable.id, id)).returning();\n  if (!row) { res.status(404).json({ error: \"المستخدم غير موجود\" }); return; }\n  const { passwordHash: _h, ...safeUser } = row;\n  res.json({ ...safeUser, lastActive: safeUser.lastActive?.toISOString() ?? null, createdAt: safeUser.createdAt.toISOString() });\n});\n\nexport default router;\n");
write("artifacts/api-server/src/routes/admin.ts", "import { Router } from \"express\";\nimport { writeFileSync } from \"fs\";\nimport { sql } from \"drizzle-orm\";\nimport { db, usersTable, userLogsTable, contractorsTable, itemCodeMapTable } from \"@workspace/db\";\nimport { eq, and, gte, desc } from \"drizzle-orm\";\nimport { hashPassword, verifyPassword, requireAdmin, getSeedFilePath } from \"../lib/auth-utils\";\n\nconst router = Router();\nrouter.use(requireAdmin);\n\nfunction safeUser(user: typeof usersTable.$inferSelect) {\n  const { passwordHash: _h, ...safe } = user;\n  return {\n    ...safe,\n    lastActive: safe.lastActive?.toISOString() ?? null,\n    createdAt: safe.createdAt.toISOString(),\n  };\n}\n\n/** Writes the full user list to users-seed.json so it survives fresh deployments */\nasync function writeSeedFile(): Promise<void> {\n  try {\n    const users = await db\n      .select()\n      .from(usersTable)\n      .orderBy(usersTable.createdAt);\n    const seedData = {\n      users: users.map((u) => ({\n        name: u.name,\n        loginName: u.loginName,\n        jobTitle: u.jobTitle,\n        role: u.role,\n        rawPassword: u.rawPassword ?? \"\",\n        isActive: u.isActive,\n      })),\n    };\n    writeFileSync(getSeedFilePath(), JSON.stringify(seedData, null, 2), \"utf8\");\n  } catch {\n    // Non-fatal — seed file update is best-effort\n  }\n}\n\n\nrouter.get(\"/admin/users\", async (_req, res): Promise<void> => {\n  const users = await db.select().from(usersTable).orderBy(usersTable.createdAt);\n  res.json(users.map(safeUser));\n});\n\nrouter.post(\"/admin/users\", async (req, res): Promise<void> => {\n  const { name, loginName, jobTitle, role, password } = req.body as Record<string, string>;\n  if (!name || !loginName || !password) {\n    res.status(400).json({ error: \"name, loginName, password required\" });\n    return;\n  }\n  const [row] = await db.insert(usersTable).values({\n    name, loginName, jobTitle: jobTitle || \"\", role: role || \"user\",\n    passwordHash: hashPassword(password), rawPassword: password, isActive: 1,\n  }).returning();\n  await writeSeedFile();\n  res.status(201).json(safeUser(row));\n});\n\nrouter.put(\"/admin/users/:id\", async (req, res): Promise<void> => {\n  const id = parseInt(req.params.id, 10);\n  const { name, loginName, jobTitle, string;\n  if (loginName !== undefined) updates.loginName = loginName as string;\n  if (jobTitle !== undefined) updates.jobTitle  = jobTitle as string;\n  if (role !== undefined)     updates.role      = role as string;\n  if (isActive !== undefined) updates.isActive  = Number(isActive);\n  if (password) {\n    updates.passwordHash = hashPassword(password as string);\n    updates.rawPassword  = password as string;\n  }\n  const [row] = await db.update(usersTable).set(updates).where(eq(usersTable.id, id)).returning();\n  if (!row) { res.status(404).json({ error: \"Not found\" }); return; }\n  await writeSeedFile();\n  res.json(safeUser(row));\n});\n\nrouter.delete(\"/admin/users/:id\", async (req, res): Promise<void> => {\n  const id = parseInt(req.params.id, 10);\n  const [target] = await db.select().from(usersTable).where(eq(usersTable.id, id));\n  if (!target) { res.status(404).json({ error: \"Not found\" }); return; }\n  if (target.role === \"superadmin\") {\n    res.status(403).json({ error: \"لا يمكن حذف مسؤول النظام\" });\n    return;\n  }\n  await db.delete(userLogsTable).where(eq(userLogsTable.userId, id));\n  const [row] = await db.delete(usersTable).where(eq(usersTable.id, id)).returning();\n  if (!row) { res.status(404).json({ error: \"Not found\" }); return; }\n  await writeSeedFile();\n  res.sendStatus(204);\n});\n\nrouter.get(\"/admin/users/:id/logs\", async (req, res): Promise<void> => {\n  const userId = parseInt(req.params.id, 10);\n  const sevenDaysAgo = new Date(Date.now() - 30 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);\n  const logs = await db.select().from(userLogsTable)\n    .where(and(eq(userLogsTable.userId, userId), gte(userLogsTable.loginAt, sevenDaysAgo)))\n    .orderBy(desc(userLogsTable.loginAt));\n  res.json(logs.map(l => ({ ...l, loginAt: l.loginAt.toISOString() })));\n});\n\n/**\n * DANGER: bulk-wipe BOQ items (contractors) + item code allocator.\n * Strictly does NOT touch users or user_logs — preserves all accounts.\n * Requires superadmin (via requireAdmin) AND a re-entered password.\n */\nrouter.post(\"/admin/wipe-items\", async (req, res): Promise<void> => {\n  const loginName = req.headers[\"x-admin-login\"] as string;\n  const { password } = req.body as { password?: string };\n  if (!password || typeof password !== \"string\") {\n    res.status(400).json({ error: \"كلمة المرور مطلوبة\" });\n    return;\n  }\n  const [admin] = await db.select().from(usersTable).where(eq(usersTable.loginName, loginName));\n  if (!admin || !verifyPassword(password, admin.passwordHash)) {\n    req.log.warn({ loginName }, \"wipe-items: password verification failed\");\n    res.status(401).json({ error: \"كلمة المرور غير صحيحة\" });\n    return;\n  }\n\n  let deletedContractors = 0;\n  let deletedCodes = 0;\n  try {\n    await db.transaction(async (tx) => {\n      const before = await tx.execute(sql`SELECT COUNT(*)::int AS n FROM contractors`);\n      deletedContractors = Number((before.rows[0] as { n: number }).n);\n      const beforeCodes = await tx.execute(sql`SELECT COUNT(*)::int AS n FROM item_code_map`);\n      deletedCodes = Number((beforeCodes.rows[0] as { n: number }).n);\n\n      await tx.delete(contractorsTable);\n      await tx.delete(itemCodeMapTable);\n    });\n  } catch (err) {\n    const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : \"خطأ غير معروف\";\n    req.log.error({ err: msg }, \"wipe-items: transaction failed\");\n    res.status(500).json({ error: msg });\n    return;\n  }\n\n  req.log.warn(\n    { actor: loginName, deletedContractors, deletedCodes },\n    \"wipe-items: BOQ tables cleared (users preserved)\",\n  );\n  res.json({\n    ok: true,\n    deletedContractors,\n    deletedCodes,\n    message: `تم تصفير ${deletedContractors} بند و ${deletedCodes} كود — حسابات المستخدمين سليمة`,\n  });\n});\n\nexport default router;\n");

write("artifacts/api-server/src/lib/auth-utils.ts", "import { createHash } from \"crypto\";\nimport { existsSync, readFileSync } from \"fs\";\nimport { resolve, dirname, join } from \"path\";\nimport type { Request, Response, NextFunction } from \"express\";\nimport { db, usersTable } from \"@workspace/db\";\nimport { eq } from \"drizzle-orm\";\n\nconst HASH_SALT = \"rawaf_internal_salt_2026\";\n\nexport function hashPassword(plain: string): string {\n  return createHash(\"sha256\").update(plain + HASH_SALT).digest(\"hex\");\n}\n\nexport function verifyPassword(plain: string, hash: string): boolean {\n  return hashPassword(plain) === hash;\n}\n\n/** Only superadmin can access the user-management API */\nexport async function requireAdmin(req: res.status(403).json({ error: \"Forbidden\" });\n    return;\n  }\n  next();\n}\n\n/** Resolves the api-server root directory regardless of dev vs prod */\nfunction getApiServerRoot(): string {\n  //
